Appendix
Report Period and Scope
This report is the 11th report of Mercuries Life Insurance Co., Ltd. It mainly 
discloses business development and sustainable management issues of concern to 
stakeholders in 2022 (January 1, 2022 to December 31, 2022), and some performance 
data Information will be retroactive (before 2022) or (also) extended to the most 
recent information in 2023. The geographical scope covers all bases in Taiwan (except 
for international insurance business branches), and some contents will further expand 
the scope of disclosure to partners.
Report Writing Principles
The report confirms
This report was approved by the board of directors and entrusted (PWC) to conduct 
limited confirmation on the selected key performance indicators according to 
TWSAE3000 Assurance Engagements “Other than Audits or Reviews of Historical 
Financial Information" issued by the Accounting Research and Development 
Foundation of the Republic of China (Limited Assurance), the accountant's limited 
assurance report, please refer to the appendix.
Report Issue Date
This report is issued once a year, and the content is placed on the official website of 
Mercuries Life Insurance Co., Ltd./Corporate Sustainability Zone for download and 
browsing : https://www.mli.com.tw/sites/mliportal/csr/reportdownload
Date of last issue: June 2022
Next release date: June 2024 (planned)

Appendix
管理政策
The 27th Conference of the Parties (COP27), which 
was held in Egypt in 2022, aims to keep the global 
temperature rise below 1.5ﾟC and calls for the active 
adoption of carbon reduction technologies and 
measures to cope with the increasing pace of climate 
change. In response to the impact of climate change 
and international interest in sustainability, the Financial 
Supervisory Commission launched the “Sustainable 
Development Roadmap" in January last year. Since last 
year, the Board of Directors has been overseeing the 
"GHG Inventory and Verification" schedule quarterly, 
which is not only earlier than the planning of the path 
map, but includes a company-wide greenhouse gas 
inventory in 2022 with the inventory data being verified 
by cooperative partners. In addition, the Financial 
Management Council launched the “Green Finance 
Action Plan 3.0” in September last year to continue 
promoting sustainable development and climate change 
in the financial markets and the industry as a whole, 
and to enhance the financial sector's climate resilience. 
Under the oath of international trends and domestic 
policies, we are well aware of the impact we have on our 
markets as a financial industry, and the responsibility to 
promote sustainable development and support the net 
zero transition.
In 2022, in addition to the promotion of greenhouse gas 
inventory, the Company has also established a TCFD 
mechanism for disclosure of climate-related financial 
information to disclose four management information, 
which are governance, strategy, risk management, 
indicators, and objectives. It has also formulated 
internal norms and mechanisms to regularly review and 
ensure the compliance with the “Guidance on Climate-
Related Risk and Financial Disclosure of Insurance 
Industry”. Especially in the area of external, working 
with the Life Insurance Association to develop a practice 
manual on climate-related financial disclosure for the 
domestic insurance industry to enhance the quality and 
transparency of disclosure and operational resilience; 
while in corporate governance, we have obtained 6~20% 
of the stock exchange corporate governance evaluation, 
and won extra points in the sustainable investment 
affirmation. In the aspect of information security,  the 
Company’s whole system has passed the verification of 
ISO27001: 2013 Information Management System (ISMS); 
and the verification of British Standards Institution 
BSI 10012: 2017 Personal Information Management 
System (PIMS) ; with respect to social responsibility, the 
company's micro insurance has been praised by the 
FSC for eight consecutive years, and was awarded the 
"Business Excellence Award" and the "Care Award for 
Physical and Mental Disabilities" in 2022 by providing 
basic insurance protection for elderly people with the 
Small Amount Whole Life Insurance, and also receives 
the “Performance Excellence Award” from FSC in aging 
insurance competition. Moreover, the Company has also 
newly added and optimized its online functions, with 
new contract action coverage rate reached by 97.96%. 
Heeded the call of the Government's efforts to support 
the arts and culture industry, we also sponsor the Taiwan 
Lantern Festival and the exhibition of artists' works in 
2023.
The relocation of our corporate headquarters to Neihu 
in 2022 marks a new milestone for our company after 
the first office building in Taichung with green building 
label. Under the trend of pursuing financial innovation 
and technological innovation and expanding digital 
services, "A Word of Promise, A Friend for Life" has 
always been our service spirit. Based on this, we always 
uphold the care of every policyholder who becomes a 
good friend with us since inception, and the business 
sustainability is also our original intention kept in mind. 
In the near future, Mercuries Life Insurance will be“Focus 
on Operation and Steady Growth” is our main axis of 
middle and long-term operation, with the five major 
strategies of ”sound finance, expertized channel, digital 
transformation, highlighted brand, win customers” 
for continuous cultivation, and be ready for the next 
thirty years. We aspire to be experts in guaranteed and 
investment goods, working with all stakeholders to make 
the world a better place through our efforts.
A Message from the Chairman
Chairman, Mercuries Life Insurance Co., Ltd    
Wong, Chau-Shi

Sustainable high performance in 2022 
Stable financial structure
◆ Total premium income reached NT$114.93billion.
◆ Net loss after tax reached NT$ 13.659 billion.
Ethical management
◆ Ranked Top 6% - 20% Stock Exchange Corporate 
Governance Index.
◆ Listed in the "Taiwan RAFI® EMP 99 Index” of the 
Taiwan Stock Exchange.
◆ System-wide passed the verification of ISO27001: 2013 
Information Management System (ISMS); passed the \
     verification of British Standards Institution BSI 10012: 2017 
Personal Information Management System (PIMS).
◆ Optimized the law change management system to 
strengthen the law change management and effectively 
improve the law compliance culture.
◆ Conducted ethical management education and training, 
including directors, internal and field staffs, in order to 
implement the concept of ethical management.
Reinforcement of communication between 
stakeholders
◆ Convened the physical shareholders' meeting 
supplemented by the video auxiliary platform, whereby 
the shareholders avoid the risk of group gathering during 
the epidemic and participate in the shareholders' meeting 
online.
Responsible investment
◆ The attendance ratio of shareholders' meetings of listed 
companies reached 98.55%, exceeding the insurance 
industry target of 70% set by the competent authority.
Corporate 
Corporate 
Governance
Governance
Highlighted Brand through social initiatives
◆ More than NT$ 50.09 million has been invested in 
public welfare, and the number of people benefited 
reached more than 210,000.
◆ A total of 763 volunteers worked for 3 hours each time, 
which amounted to about 2,289 hours.
Fair Customer Treatment
◆ The number of persons with disabilities insured in 2022 
increases by 0.09% over the previous year.
◆ Continued to launch the "Loan Preferential Rate Project 
for Economically Vulnerable Rescue” in 2022 to help the 
insured households in trouble overcome difficulties and 
extend the application period for six months to ease the 
economic pressure of the insured households. By the 
end of December 2022, the total number of applicants 
was 167 persons /194 cases, with a total loan amount 
reached NT$ 13,841,877.
◆ 	The claim settlement rate using Consortium Blockchain 
or Medical Union increased by 65.34%.
◆ Added and optimized the online operation, with the 
action insurance rate under New Insurance Contract 
reached 97.96%. 
◆ The growth rate of automated service population 
reached 7.02%.
◆ 	Micro insurance had been recognized by the FSC for 
eight consecutive years, and was awarded the “Business 
Excellence Award” and “Care Award for Persons with 
Physical and Mental Disabilities” in 2022.
◆ Provided basic insurance protection for elderly people 
with small old-age insurance, and also received the 
“Performance Excellence Award” from FSC in 2022.
Caring for employees
◆ Implemented “Talent Inventory” among colleagues and 
supervisors at specific levels, and arranged all levels of 
management to understand the status of talent 
reserves.
◆ Continued to promote succession planning and 
strengthened leadership courses for executives by 
selecting 60 to 70 middle and senior executives to 
participate in the plan, and cultivate potential and 
developmental successors.
◆ Total investment for internal training cost exceeded NT$ 
7.31 million, the total training hours exceeded 50,000 
hours, and the average training hours per capita were 
about 28.51 hours.
◆ Total investment for field training cost exceeded 
NT$ 23.45 million, the total training hours 
exceeded350,676 hours, and the average training 
hours per capita were about36.52 hours.
◆ New colleague shall obtain the certificate of life 
insurance agents, and the pass rate was 68.5%, which 
was better than the industry average of 39.6%.
Sustainable environment
◆The company will reduce the total carbon emissions by 
50.41% from 2016 to 2022.
◆Obtained ISO14001 Environmental Management 
System.
◆	Acquisition of Greenhouse Gas Inventory 
Confidence Report.

Sustainable 
Version

In accordance with the sustainability standards at home and abroad, as 
well as the continuous promotion of various policies and measures by 
the competent authorities, Mercuries Life Insurance actively promotes 
ESG and sustainable governance, and deepens the development 
of sustainable finance. Besides, in combination with the corporate 
sustainable development policy and five capital inputs, Mercuries Life 
Insurance also sets its annual sustainable development goals to manage 
the economic, environmental and social risks and impacts, and respond 
to the global sustainable development trend, thus to become the most 
value-creating professional life insurance company.

Company Profile
Note: Total capital is consistent with the announcement of paid-in capital and general corporate 
bonds on the Market Observation Post System..
Since the establishment in 1993, Mercuries Life Insurance has been engaging in the life 
insurance business and was publicly listed in Taiwan Stock Exchange on December 18, 2012. 
With investment-linked and protection products as the main commodity strategy, the Company 
also adheres to the five major strategies of ”Sound Finance, Expertized Channel, Digital 
Transformation, Highlighted Brand and Winning Customers” for continuous cultivation, with 
“Focus on Operation and Steady Growth” as the main axis of middle- and long-term operation 
to pursue a sustainable development.

Appendix
Mercuries Life Insurance shows the determination of 
sustainable development with the brand spirit of "A Word 
of Promise, A Friend for Life". We take the initiative to 
follow domestic and foreign sustainable regulations such 
as UN SDGs, UNGC, ISO26000, TCFD, SASB, and Sustainable 
Development Best Practice Principles for TWSE/TPEx Listed 
Companies, and consider issues exclusive to the financial 
insurance industry such as responsible investment, fair 
customer treatment, anti-money laundering and counter 
terrorism financing, FinTech innovation, in combination 
with the corporate social responsibility policy and five 
major capital investments, to establish the annual 
ESG goal and pay attention to ESG related problems, 
thereby responding to the global trend for sustainable 
development and becoming the most value-creating 
professional life insurance company.
Sustainable Development 
Management
Based on “Mercuries Life Insurance Co., Ltd. Corporate 
Social Responsibility Policy”, Mercuries Life Insurance draws 
up the “Mercuries Life Insurance Co., Ltd. Corporate Social 
Responsibility Best Practice Principles” in accordance with 
the “Sustainable Development Best Practice Principles for 
TWSE/TPEx Listed Companies” jointly formulated by the 
Stock Exchange and the Securities OTC Trading Center, so 
as to manage the Company's economic, environmental 
and social risks and impacts. The Executive Office under 
the General Manager is authorized to be responsible for the 
planning and execution of policies, systems, management 
approaches and action plans, so as to promote the relevant 
issues of sustainable development, as well as to summarize 
the internal annual investment results and prepare CSR 
report, which shall be submitted to the Board of Directors 
for issuance, and exposed on the Market Observation Post 
System, and official website of stock exchange, thereby 
presenting the efforts for sustainable development.

Appendix
Establishment of Sustainable Business Objective
The Board of Directors convenes ordinary meetings on a monthly basis to lead the major decisions 
and business directions of the Company, including topics related to the economy, environment 
and society, as well as to review the execution outcome, draw up the annual business plan at the 
end of the year, and outline the strategic blueprint of the Company for the whole year. The General 
Manager reports the Company’s annual plan implementation status in the Board meetings on 
a quarterly basis, to review the indicators and grasp the Company's business objectives and 
direction.
In order to strengthen the management of the Company's sustainable development, and by 
the end of 2022, the "Corporate Sustainability Group" composed of departments originally 
involved in preparation of the sustainable report will be adjusted and established in terms of its 
organizational structure and implementation contents. The general manager will serve as the 
convenor, and the office of the Chief executive of the corporate sustainability secretary unit will 
be responsible for communication and integration. Besides, the corporate sustainability group is 
divided into environmental group, social group and corporate governance group, of which, the 
corporate sustainability group plans to hold quarterly meetings to track the implementation of the 
Company's sustainable development and report to the board of directors regularly every year.

Appendix
Attach importance to corporate governance
Protect the rights and interests of shareholders, strengthen 
the functions of the Board of Directors, respect the rights 
and interests of stakeholders, and enhance the information 
transparency.
◆ Listen to shareholders and provide transparent 
disclosure.
◆ Conduct the Board performance appraisal and enhance 
the Board effectiveness.
◆ Implement the ethical management, education and 
training.
◆ Sound financial structure, pursue the growth and profit.
Implement the ethical management
Issue the Codes of Ethical Management to prohibit all forms 
of dishonest conduct and set up the reporting boxes and 
accusation line to prevent the corruption and malpractice.
Implement the fair customer treatment principle
Abide by the fair customer treatment principle, pay attention 
to the customer experience, and protect the rights and 
interests of policyholders.
◆ Implement the financial consumer protection in line 
with regulations.
◆ Provide the financial friendly services, and care for the 
vulnerable groups.
◆ Carry out the educational training; enhance the 
professionalism of agency force to provide the high-
quality service.
Care for employees
Comply with relevant labor laws and create a safe and equal 
working environment with diversity and inclusiveness.
◆ Sound salary and welfare system to provide the 
employees with career development opportunities.
◆ Hold regular labor and management meetings to build 
good employment relations.
◆ Enact the human rights policies, ensure the equal pay for 
equal work, and create a gender-equal workplace.
◆ Pay attention to employee's physical and mental 
health, encourage exercise, provide stress massage, and 
organize the employee caring activities.
Engage in social participation
Participate in the sport events for a long time and encourage 
the employees to be volunteers.
◆ Support the financial insurance education and advocate 
the risk awareness.
◆ Promote the sports and healthy life for all.
◆ Invest in community services and exert the influence.
Promote sustainable environment
Decrease the impact of climate change on the environment to 
achieve environmental sustainability.
◆ 100% local suppliers to reduce the carbon footprint.
◆ Actively promote e-service to reduce the consumption of 
natural resources as papers.
◆ Set the carbon reduction targets and implement.
◆ Invest the green industry and pay attention to 
environment topics.
Sustainable Development Policy
The Company has established the “Mercuries Life Insurance Co., Ltd. Sustainable 
Development Policy” by resolution of the Board of Directors, so as to create the 
greatest value for stakeholders such as policyholders, employees and shareholders 
based on the information disclosure of corporate governance, environmental 
sustainability, social welfare participation and corporate sustainability. Mercuries 
Life Insurance also dedicates to the implementation of sustainable development 
by spontaneously following the UN SDGs, including "Decent Work and Economic 
Growth", "Good Health and Well-being", "Gender Equality", "No Poverty", "Quality 
Education", "Responsible Consumption and Production" and "Climate Action". 
Through the promotion of sustainability organization and policy, the Company 
makes the sustainability management commitment consistent, and achieves the 
vision of "the most value-creating professional life insurance company".

Appendix
Major topics management
This report has been prepared in accordance with the 
general, industrial and major topic guidelines published 
by the Global Reporting Initiatives (GRI) and follows nine 
major requirements and eight guidelines.rofessional life 
insurance company.
Engagement Process
Mercuries Life Insurance has developed a list of 18 
sustainable topics based on competent authorities' 
concerns and strategies at home and abroad. It also 
invites all department heads to assess the internal, 
external, actual and potential impacts of the sustainable 
topics. In addition, 10 major themes were identified by 
referring to the concerns of external stakeholders, which 
were approved by the corporate sustainability group, 
with positive and negative impact assessments being 
conducted on these grounds.
The Executive Office defines the report boundary and 
contents by comparing the materiality matrix and GRI 
Standards topics, and then relevant data provided by each 
department is further compiled into the corporate social 
responsibility report. After the third-party guarantees 
and submission to the Board of Directors, the report is 
available for download by all stakeholders. Subsequently, 
the Executive Office still coordinates among departments 
to continuously collect information and track stakeholder 
engagement through internal and external channels.
Analyze the topics 
concerned stakeholders 
through a questionnaire 
downloaded from the 
official website.
Identify the internal 
and external impact 
of topics through 
internal questionnaires 
and discussion, and 
form the materiality 
matrix together with 
the results of external 
questionnaire analysis.
The general manager 
serves as the chairman 
to determine ten 
major issues and 
issues of concern to 
stakeholders.
Continue to collect in-
formation and track 
stakeholders' engage-
ment through internal 
and external channels.

Standards topics to 
determine the report 
boundary and content.

Significance degree of sustainability topic
Mercuries Life Insurance evaluates 'actual 'and 'potential' positive and negative impacts through 
'likelihood' and 'impact scale'. The "positive significance" and "negative significance" of each topic 
are calculated, and the total score of the impact degree of each topic is obtained by summing 
up the absolute value scores, and then sorted according to the total score of "impact degree”. 
Finally, the corporate sustainability group discusses and decides on ten major topics: ethical 
management, business performance, employee compensation and welfare, risk management, 
corporate governance, information security, compliance with laws, digital finance and innovation, 
fair hospitality and customer experience, climate change response and environmental management.

Appendix

Decent work 
and economic 
growth
Corresponding 
SDGS▼
Sustainable 
Governance
To establish a good corporate governance system, Mercuries Life 
Insurance has formulated “Mercuries Life Insurance Code of Practice 
on Corporate Governance” in strict accordance with the “Code of 
Practice on Insurance Corporate Governance” and “Sustainable 
Development Best Practice Principles for TWSE/TPEx Listed 
Companies”, establish an effective corporate governance structure, 
pay attention to capital adequacy, asset quality, operation and 
management ability, profitability, asset liquidity and risk sensitivity, 
follow laws and regulations and improve internal management, 
protect shareholders' rights and interests, strengthen the function 
of the board of directors, protect the rights and interests of the 
guarantor and respect the interests of stakeholders, maintain 
liquidity and improve information transparency, so as to achieve 
sustainable operation.

Total assets of NT$ 1,458.233 billion, net loss after tax of NT$ 13.659 billion, and total 
premium income of NT$ 114.93 billion. 
Rated top 6%~20% in Corporate Governance Evaluation by Taiwan Stock Exchange
Held the entity shareholders' meeting, supplemented with TOCC auxiliary platform, to 
strengthen communication with stakeholders. 
Set up the home office environment for employees and strengthened the home office asset 
security control; passed system-wide ISO27001: 2013 Information Security Management 
System(ISMS) verification; passed the verification of the British Standards Institute BSI 
10012:2017 Personal Information Management System (PIMS); qualified rate of all the 
internal staff in the information security advocacy course reached 100%;participated in 
the F-SOC to enhance the quality of financial security monitoring through sharing and 
communication among financial institutions 
Conducted dishonest conduct risk assessment project, analyzed and evaluated business 
activities with high risk of dishonest conduct in the business area, and analyzed and 
reviewed accordingly.
Optimized the law change management system to strengthen the law change management 
and effectively improve the law compliance culture. 
Optimized the money laundering and terrorism risk assessment mechanism and anti-money 
laundering system functions. 
2023 Goals
◆  Complete and expand BS 10012:2017 Personal Information Management System (PIMS) 
verification to the whole company. 
◆  Continuously carry out ISO27001:2013 Information Security Management System (ISMS) 
verification, to maintain certificate validity. 
◆  Handle the maturity assessment of capital security management, establish a self-
assessment mechanism, and continue to deepen and implement capital security 
management. 
◆  Introduce ISO22301 Operation Continuity Management System to strengthen the 
resilience of financial services. 
◆  Conduct compliance risk assessment (CRA), including compliance risk assessment report 
and risk improvement plan, propose the weaknesses of compliance risk management 
and supervise the improvement plan and schedule for the whole company operation 
situation. 
◆  Improve the integrity and correctness of the stakeholder management system database, 
and implement the stakeholder transaction control mechanism. 
◆  Conduct quality assurance (QA) for compliance, assist and supervise business units to 
identify and manage compliance risks. 
◆  Expand the effectiveness of anti-money laundering system and enhance the awareness of 
employees.

Operational Performance
Mercuries Life Insurance ranked 10th in 2022 with first 
year premium of NT$29.602 billion and total premium of 
NT$114.93 billion, ranking 7th in cumulative terms. By the 
end of 2022, the Company’s total assets reached NT$1.46 
trillion, owners' equity reached NT$28.848 billion and 
operating income reached NT$109.647 billion, resulting in 
a net loss after tax of NT$13.659 billion, and net loss per 
share after tax of NT$4.34.
As overall operating environment is extremely challenging, 
the Company implements asset activation and plans to 
increase operating capital, including cash capital increase, 
real estate activation, asset redistribution, disposal of 
invested equity, introduction of strategic investors, etc., 
to facilitate the adjustment of investment layout and 
allocation, and at the same time contribute positively 
to the capital adequacy ratio and net worth ratio. 
Furthermore, the Company is with its concerted effort to 
implement  the sustainable management, thus achieving 
its goal of improving operation efficiency and sound 
management.

Corporate Governance
This Company has actively promoted the corporate governance, and 
also has received the honor of being rated top 6%~20% in the Corporate 
Governance Evaluation by Taiwan Stock Exchange for eight consecutive 
years.
Corporate Governance Structure

A total of 10 seats of directors have been established for the Board of Directors with the 
term of office of 3 years, of which 4 are the professional natural person directors, and 3 
independent directors are all initially elected. And in 2022, 19 sessions of the Board of 
Directors’ meetings have been held, with the overall attendance rate of 97.16%.
Audit Committee

Corporate Governance and 
Nomination Committee
We have established the “Standard Operating Procedures for Handling Directors' 
Requests” to assist the directors in performing their duties, and the Board of Directors 
appointed the Deputy General Manger, Jade Tien, of the Executive Office to act as the 
corporate governance supervisor, whose main duties include “handling the matters 
relating to the Board of Directors’ meetings and shareholders’ meetings pursuant to 
laws”, “preparing the meeting minutes of Board of Directors’ meetings and shareholders’ 
meetings”, “assisting in on-boarding and continuing education of directors”, “providing 
documents required for business executed by directors” and “assisting directors with 
regulatory compliance” as well as building a perfect communication bridge between the 
Board of Directors and the management team.

Appendix
Directors selection
The Company has set a Corporate Governance and 
Nomination Committee since 2020.  In accordance with 
the “Mercuries Life Insurance Methods for Election of 
Directors”, the standards of professional knowledge, 
technology, experience and gender diversity and 
independence of the members of the Board of Directors 
are thereby formulated to  identify, vet and nominate 
candidates for directors and senior managers. In 
nominating the list of independent director candidates, 
shall pay attentions to the qualifications, professionalism, 
integrity of the nominees and the fact that they are also 
directors, supervisors, committee members or chairmen 
of other companies, with a view to meeting the long-
term interests of shareholders. The nominated director 
candidates shall be elected by the Board of Directors 
through resolution and proposed by the shareholders' 
committee. 
Diversity of Board Members
The current board of directors of our company has 
10 members, including 3 independent directors, 
accounting for 33%, and 1 female director, accounting 
for 10%. The average age of board members as a whole 
is 65.1, of which, the Board of Directors consisted of 1 
member between the age of 40 (inclusive) - 50 years 
old, accounted for 10%; 2 members between the age 
of 50 (inclusive) - 60 years old, accounted for 20%; and 
7 members above the age of 60 (inclusive) years old, 
accounted for 70%.We have six professional directors, 
who are equipped with the background and professional 
knowledge of the fields of operation management, 
legal, financial and accounting, investment and risk 
management etc., consistent with the principle of board 
diversity.

Appendix
Customized Trainings for the 
Board of Directors
In order to promote the directors to improve their 
professional knowledge, in accordance with the Taiwan 
Stock Exchange's “Guidelines for Education for Directors 
and Supervisors of Listed Companies” and “Mercuries Life 
Insurance Directors' Training Method”, the Company is 
supported by the Corporate Governance and Nomination 
Committee to plan the annual director education and 
training program, which will be revised in 2021 to take into 
account the results of the Board's performance evaluation, 
ensure that the directors have the professional knowledge 
of the core curriculum of the Director Education Map, 
as well as assist the beginning directors to understand 
the Company's operating conditions, including the 
introduction of industry and internal organization, the 
director's basic legal responsibilities and other courses.
The directors of our company attach importance to further 
study to enhance professional knowledge. In 2022, the 
total number of training hours is 145.5, of which, the 
average training hours for each director is 14.6 hours 
(Stock Exchange prescribes 6 hours for directors of listed 
companies). Topics include fair hospitality and financial 
consumer protection, international anti-corruption and 
whistleblower protection, money laundering prevention, 
ESG sustainable management, the impact of IFSR17/ICS 
on commodities, international climate change trends and 
practical case analysis, information security, etc.
Management on independence of 
directors and conflict of interest

The Company has three independent directors and 
formulated the "Rules on Scope of Duties of Independent 
Directors", stipulating that "Any objections or reservations 
of independent directors shall be stated in the Board 
Minutes", "The Company shall not obstruct, refuse or 
circumvent the performance of business by independent 
directors", "When deemed necessary by independent 
directors to perform business, the Board may be asked 
to appoint relevant personnel or hire their own experts 
to assist”. The independence of independent directors 
is examined annually in accordance with the "Measures 
for the Establishment of Independent Directors and 
Matters to be Followed by Public Issuing Companies". 
Both the Company and the independent directors issued 
a statement and set up the "Prevention Mechanism 
for Conflict of Interest in Domestic Equity Commodity 
Investment" to avoid the conflict of interest with the 
Company's investment or other behaviors that adversely 
affect the Company's goodwill or interests. The declaration 
is signed by all the directors.
In accordance with the rules of Procedures for the Board 
of Directors of the Company, the directors, who have an 
interest in themselves or the legal person they represent, 
shall not join in the discussion or vote the next time when 
the Board of Directors explains an important content of 
the interest, especially if it is harmful to the interests of 
the Company, shall withdraw from the discussion and 
vote, and not exercise their voting rights on behalf of other 
directors. Any spouse or second relative of a director, or 
any company with which the director has a controlling 
affiliation, who has an interest in any matter at the meeting 
shall be deemed to have an interest of his own in such 
matter.
Board of Directors and Functional 
Committee Performance 
Evaluation
According to the Mercuries Life Insurance Board 
Performance Evaluation Method, the Corporate 
Governance and Nominating Committee shall conduct 
an annual internal performance evaluation of the Board 
and functional committees and an external performance 
evaluation every three years. Taiwan Corporate Governance 
Association will be appointed in 2023 to evaluate the 
performance of the board of directors from December 1, 
2021 to November 30, 2022.
In 2022, the internal performance evaluation results of 
the Board of Directors, Audit Committee, Remuneration 
Committee, Risk Management Committee, Corporate 
Governance and Nomination Committee all reached 
"excellent", indicating that the functions and operational 
efficiency of the Board of Directors are implemented and 
brought into full play.
Board performance evaluation focuses on ESG issues such 
as "corporate governance", to promote the formulation of 
corporate governance measures, support the Company 
to participate in stock exchange’s corporate governance 
evaluation, and fully protect the shareholders' rights and 
interests. In addition, the Board of Directors also actively 
promotes the fair customer treatment culture, provides 
the quality customer service, establishes the performance 
goals in business plans, supervises the implementation of 
the management team, and continuously strengthens the 
operational efficiency of the Board of Directors based on 
the results of the performance evaluation of the Board of 
Directors, improves the corporate governance culture, and 
actively promotes the vision of sustainable development.
The performance evaluation results of the Board of 
Directors of the Company shall be used as a reference for 
the selection or nomination of directors; the performance 
evaluation results of individual directors shall be used as 
the reference basis for determining their individual salaries 
and remuneration. The remuneration committee may 
make recommendations to the Corporate Governance and 
Nomination Committee on the indicators and contents of 
the performance evaluation.

Remuneration Policy

According to the Articles of Association of the Company, the 
remuneration of directors (including independent directors) 
shall be authorized by the board of directors according 
to their participation degrees and contribution values in 
operation of the Company and the usual level of industry.
The remuneration policy for managers shall be based on 
factors such as job title, work experience, price inflation 
and market level, which shall reflect performance and be 
competitive; Review the remuneration system at any time 
according to the actual operating conditions and relevant 
laws and regulations, and give reasonable remuneration 
after comprehensive consideration of the current trend of 
corporate governance, so as to strike a balance between 
sustainable operation and risk control of the company. 
The Company has set up a compensation committee 
composed of three independent directors. According to 
the "Compensation Management Measures for Directors 
and Managers", the Company regularly reviews the 
compensation policies and systems of directors and 
managers in a professional and objective position and 
puts forward suggestions to the board of Directors. The 
compensation principles are as follows: 1. When performing 
the functions and powers, the performance evaluation 
and compensation of directors and managers shall refer 
to the usual level of industry, and consider a rationality 
of the correlation with individual performance, company 
operating performance and future risks; 2. Directors and 
managers should not be guided to pursue compensation 
and engage in activities beyond the risk scope of the 
Company; 3. Performance appraisal and remuneration 
standards or structures shall be established based on future 
risk-adjusted performance and in line with the Company's 
overall long-term profits and shareholders' interests; 4. The 
payment of remuneration should be timed to match future 
risk-adjusted earnings to avoid undue losses after payment 
of remuneration. A significant proportion of remuneration 
should be paid in deferred or equity-related form if any; 5. 
When assessing the contribution of directors and managers 
to the Company's profits, a holistic analysis of the insurance 
industry should be conducted to determine whether such 
profits are due to the utilization of the Company's overall 
advantages, such as the lower cost of capital, in order to 
effectively assess their contributions. 
Salary remuneration includes cash remuneration, stock 
options, dividend shares, retirement benefits or severance 
payments, various allowances and other measures with 
substantial incentives; Its scope must be consistent with 
that of director and manager remuneration recorded in the 
guidelines for annual performance of the public company. 
In discussing the recommendations of 
this Committee, the Board of Directors 
shall take into account such matters as 
the amount of remuneration, the method 
of payment and the future risks of the 
Company.

Equal Treatment of Shareholder Rights

This Company values the interests and rights of every shareholder and treats all 
shareholders equally. Through the interactions from orientation meeting and 
shareholders' meeting, the shareholders' meeting, by means of electronic voting, 
makes the exercise of the shareholders' rights and interests free from the limitation 
of time and space, and further protect the shareholders' rights and interests. In 2022, 
the shareholders’ meeting was often held with the help of video form, and in response 
to the epidemic, the shareholders can report online, vote, ask questions, and watch 
the live broadcast of the meeting; Investor and shareholder contact information is 
also provided on the company website to ensure that investors are fully informed of 
important company information.

Appendix
Promotion of Ethical 
Management

In order to establish the corporate culture and sound 
development of ethical management, and establish 
a good business structure, the Board of Directors 
has approved the formulation of "Code of Ethical 
Management" and "Ethical Management Operation 
Procedure and Behavior Management Policy". All 
forms of dishonest behavior, including improper gifts 
or entertainments, are prohibited, and the Company 
has the "Operation Method for Accepting Gifts and 
Entertainment", which stipulates that any person who 
receives the gifts or entertainments valued at more 
than NT$3,000 or cannot be evaluated objectively, shall 
immediately report to the Headquarters Regulatory 
Compliance Office. The complaint e-mail address 
shall be set, so that any person who has objective 
evidence and reasonable belief that any employee of 
the Company is involved in any crime, malpractice or 
violation of laws or regulations while performing his/
her duties may be reported. According to evaluations 
from the head office and its subsidiaries, there was no 
incident related to honest operation involving fraud, 
insider trading, anti-competitive behavior, anti-trust and 
monopoly behavior, as well as market manipulation in 
2022. 
Complaint System

In order to establish an honest and transparent 
corporate culture and promote the sound operation 
of the company, the Company has formulated the 
“Handling Measures for Complaint Cases" and set up a 
special complaint mailbox. Furthermore, On December 
22, 2022, the "Handling Measures for Complaint Cases" 
was revised, and a special telephone line was added 
as the complaint channel for internal and external 
personnel use, and the Company has also designated 
the compliance unit of head office as its special unit 
responsible for accepting complaint cases. 
The Company's complaint channel is set up to promote 
its sound operation and protect the informer. For the 
cases that are not accepted by the complaint mailbox, 
but can be judged to belong to other specialized 
units of the Company according to such complaint 
content, the Company has set up complaint center 
and service quality department and other specialized 
units independent of the channel to handle the cases, 
and has also formulated relevant norms and operating 
procedures. Based on the Company's external integrity 
and to protect the rights and interests of customers, 
the Law Compliance Office will assist in transferring to 
relevant units for processing. 
In 2022, no complaint cases were reported through the 
complaint channel and accepted. 
Other cases received from the complaint mailbox in 2022 
are as follows: 
(1)Transfer to other business unit: 15 cases were 
transferred to the complaint center, business support 
department, service quality department, human 
resources department and other units for processing 
according to contents of complains. 
(2)others : cases were unable to be identified with object 
or incident, can not be processed, and just stored for 
reference. 
Commitment of Anti-Corruption

The directors and all the agency force of the 
Company have signed the ethical management policy 
statement, and the contractors are required to sign the 
"Commitment of Anti-corruption".
And the domestic equity commodity investment interest 
conflict prevention mechanism is formulated, so the 
Company’s domestic equity commodity investment 
related personnel shall ensure to execute the business 
based on the client's interests, fulfill their faithful good 
faith principle, to avoid the conflict with the Company's 
investment interests or other behaviors adversely 
affecting the Company's reputation or interests; relevant 
staff need to sign the declaration, and the Company 
directors also 100% sign.
Implementation of Regulatory 
Compliance

It shall set up a regulatory compliance unit subordinate 
to the General Manager, responsible for the planning, 
management and implementation of the regulatory 
compliance system, and set up a regulatory compliance 
officer of the head office, to generally manage the 
regulatory compliance business, report the regulatory 
compliance issues to the Board of Directors and Audit 
Committee at least semiannually, and actively conduct 
the regulatory compliance educational training and 
advocacy. This includes conducting the business 
advocacy of regulatory compliance to senior executives 
at monthly management meetings, and holding the 
quarterly seminars for corporate regulatory compliance 
executives to deeply cultivate the culture of regulatory 
compliance.
In order to improve the real-time and effectiveness 
of regulatory changes and strengthen the tracking 
and management procedures of regulatory changes, 
the Company introduced the regulatory change 
management system in 2021, and then improved 
the system in 2022 and optimized functions such as 
"Significance Mark on Law Change" and "Internal 
Regulation Management Interface and Report", 
etc. Through the automatic system, the Company

Improvement in Quality of Agents 
Recruitment

Regarding the notification of agent violation, the 
Company will review and investigate the agent's 
behavior according to the investigation evidence, and 
submit to inventory or list the agent and stakeholder 
according to the further review and evaluation of the 
case, so as to proactively safeguard the rights and 
interests of potential disputed customers and avoid the 
infringement of customer rights and interests. In order to 
implement the Principle of Complaint and Protection for 
fair customer treatment, we should strengthen the policy 
of "strengthening management of agent complained by 
customers". At the same time, the list of former reported 
agents and communication offices will be provided for 
reference by business management units, to strengthen 
the supervision of former reported salesmen and 
communication offices, implement the risk prevention 
and data as management measures for agents, thus 
improve the quality of agents recruitment and safeguard 
the rights and interests of policyholders.
In order to improve the management of agents, the 
review team was set up in 2021 to review the cases 
involving the agent recruitment violations (referred to 
as the "Review Team"), which will serve as the review 
and decision organization for cases involving the agents 
violation behavior of Item 1 of Article 19 of the Rules 
Governing Insurance agents or other major violations. 
In addition to the Regulatory Affairs Office, Regulatory 
Compliance Office, district and business management 
related offices, the team members shall include the 
agents representative, to maintain the independence 
and equity of agents violation case review, and protect 
the working rights and interests of agents.
Sanction and Improvement

In 2022, there were two corrections by the Insurance 
Bureau of the Financial Regulatory Commission, 
and there was no penalty amount. The amount of 
penalty imposed by the Labor Protection Bureau was 
NT$5,721,296 in 2022, and the amount of penalty 
corrected by the Insurance Bureau of Financial 
Super visor y Commission was NT$5,843,900 in 
2021. Deficiencies in both years were improved by 
implementing the follow-up improvement measures.
Sanction
Improvement
Management of the core business of investmenttype insurance commercial products, 
for insured customers who have increased risk, did not provide an abstract of the 
proposal after the increase.
The operation process has been adjusted, and for policyholders who have 
undergone a risk increase, a summary form of the proposal after the increase 
is provided.
The customer risk attribute analysis question paper is poorly defined.
The customer risk attribute analysis 
questionnaire has been revised.
The source of funds for policyholders to pay insurance premiums is loans or insurance 
policy borrowings, and the purchase of insurance products with policy value reserves, 
the content of telephone interviews is not complete.
The preunderwriting call 
template has been revised. 
The dispute over the wages of labor insurance insurance is mainly due to the issue of 
the determination of the salary of the agents.
In order to improve the welfare of colleagues in the field, starting from July 
2020, the contracting and service remuneration for new sales of policy 
products have been included in the insurance salary range, with a view to 
creating a better working environment for colleagues.

of "sanction list + major criminal involved + self-

Internal Control and Audit
The Company has established the 
internal audit unit under the Board of 
Directors to perform the audit service 
based on the principle of independence. 
The internal audit unit provides 
assistance to the Board of Directors and 
senior management in auditing and 
assessing whether the risk management 
and internal control system are operated 
effectively, and to timely provide 
improvement recommendations to 
ensure the effectiveness of the internal 
control system. The internal audit unit 
shall conduct a general audit on the 
financial, business, information and 
other management units at least once 
a year, and conduct the item audit 
according to the actual needs, so as to 
reduce the risks of various operations. 
The internal audit unit will continue to 
track the incomplete improvement of 
each unit until it is completed.
The scope of internal audit includes the 
head office and branch offices. Auditors 
handle the internal audit, which can be 
divided into the "general audit", "item 
audit" and "audit designated by the 
competent authority". General and item 
audits are carried out by auditors in 
accordance with the annual audit plan; 
the audit designated by the competent 
authority shall be carried out according 
to the instructions of the competent 
authority.
The audit unit carries out the general 
audit every year according to the audit 
plan, and the sampling method is based 
on the risk level of the operation item of 
each department to be audited.
Each department or office of the 
Company shall implement the self-
audit periodically at least once annually, 
and shall perform the item self-audit 
according to the actual needs. When 
each department or office is performing 
the self-audit, the self-audit supervisor 
shall designate personnel other than 
the original case handlers to execute 
the self-audit according to the specified 
audit content, and shall also fulfill the 
non-disclosure obligation in advance. 
Each department or office shall establish 
the “Audit Items” according to its scope 
of business, and shall also adjust such 
items according to the actual business 
condition at the end of each year.

internal control three-line of defense

operation of the internal control

Chief Information Security Officer of 
the Company jointly issue the “Internal

and submit to the Board of Directors for 
approval, followed by announcement 
under the “Public Interests and Other 
Issues” of the Public Information on the 
Company’s website.

Risk Management
Risk Management Framework

The Board of Directors is the highest decision-making unit of the Company to establish an effective 
risk management system, and takes the ultimate responsibility for overall risk management. The 
Board of Directors shall make decisions according to the overall business environment and strategy, 
and ensure the effective operation of risk management mechanism. The Board of Directors has 
a risk management committee, currently composed of 5 directors (including all independent 
directors), and the independent director serves as the convenor, responsible for formulating the 
risk management policies and procedures, implementing the risk management decisions of the 
Board of Directors, and reporting the overall risk management operation to the Board of Directors 
quarterly, as well as managing all kinds of risks and establishing the management indicators, and 
coordinating the interaction and communication of risk management functions across units. With 
the approval of the Board of Directors, a risk controller is appointed to be responsible for the overall 
risk management of the Company. And the Risk Management Department is set to take charge of 
daily risk monitoring, measurement, evaluation and other executive affairs of the Company and 
exercise its powers independently from business units.
Risk Management Three-Line of Defense
Risk Management Policy

We formulate the "Risk Management Policy" in 
accordance with the "Insurance Industry Internal 
Control and Audit System Implementation Measures" 
and "Insurance Industry Risk Management Code of 
Practice" issued by the FSC and approved by the 
Board of Directors, whose main contents include 
the risk management objectives and strategies, 
organizational structure and responsibilities, risk 
management principles and risk management 
procedures, etc. Risk management policy shall 
be implemented after submitted to the Board of 
Directors for approval, and the Board of Directors 
shall review it annually. In addition, there are the 
"Asset Risk Management Method", "Asset and 
Liability with Risk Management Method", "Liability 
Risk Management Method", "Capital Adequacy 
Risk Management Method" and "Operation Risk 
Management Method" to assess and manage 
various risks of the Company. In 2022, "climate risk" 
management was included in the "Risk Management 
Policy", and "Climate Risk Management Measures" 
were formulated and implemented.
Risk Identification and 
Countermeasures

Through the process of risk identification, risk 
measurement and risk response, we comprehensively 
monitor and respond to various risks in real time, 
and make good use of close information exchange 
and communication, so as to minimize the risks. In 
addition, we also actively design the corresponding 
control mechanism for the known risks, and strive 
to establish an effective risk protection network 
by combining the professional knowledge and 
experience.

Crisis Management Mechanism

In order to prevent the occurrence of emergencies 
that may lead to the loss of the Company's reputation 
or endanger the normal operation and then cause the 
business crisis and affect the rights and interests of 
stakeholders, Mercuries Life Insurance has formulated 
the operation continuity strategy: the risk reduction 
and risk avoidance strategies are adopted to maintain 
the operation in the local/remote system backup, 
remote workplace, home office, and other modes.
In 2021, the Company conducted the internal risk 
assessment (once every two years), and identified 
the high-risk items as Pandemic diseases/system 
outage/disaster-causing earthquake, and provided 
corresponding contingency measures in the operation 
continuity plan:

In order to maintain the uninterrupted operation of the system, 
the equipment failure of the machine room was routinely 
simulated twice in 2022, while the Longtan backup system was 
also used to carry out various function tests, and all drills were 
completed in 2022. In addition, in line with the government's 
action plan to promote financial security, the Company has been 
planning the introduction of Business Continuity Management 
(BCM) since 2022, establishing the system in three stages and 
three years and achieving the certification of international 
ISO22301 standard, to strengthen its emergency response 
capacity and toughness in the face of natural disasters and other 
severe disasters, as well as maintain the normal operation and 
maintenance of the Company.
Information Security
In the Internet era, information security issues are 
becoming increasingly important. In order to implement 
the information security management, the Company 
has formulated “Information Security Policy”, “Code 
of Conduct for Information Security", and introduced 
ISO27001 information security management system, 
BS10012 personal data management system for 
relevant information security evaluation every year, 
to implement the workplace information security and 
personal data protection, reduce the risk of sensitive 
data leakage.
Governance Architecture for 
Information Security 

The Company has a chief information security officer to 
take care of information security policy promotion and 
resource scheduling affairs, and also set up information 
security specialist units and supervisors, responsible 
for planning, monitoring and implementation of 
information security management operations. Each 
year, the chairman, general manager, general auditor, 
chief compliance officer for the head office  and 
information security chief jointly issue a statement of 
internal control system for the overall implementation 
of information security for the previous year and submit 
it to the board of directors for approval.
The Company has formulated the information security 
policy and information security group organization 
structure according to the functions of three levels 
"information security decision-making", "information 
security governance and management" and 
"implementation of information security operation" to 
specify relevant work responsibilities and the principles 
of power division. 
First level　Information Security Decision-Making
▶Information security decision-making group: consists 
of the general manager, the director of the information 
security department, and the directors of each system. 
▶Main work responsibilities: 
 ‧Inspect and review on direction and strategy of   
information security and personal data promotion. 
 ‧Review and audit policies and systems of information 
security and personal data. 
 ‧Decide on material events and issues of information 
security and personal data. 
 ‧Verify information security and personal
data implementation plan and results. 
Second level　Information Security Governance 
and Management
▶Information security department. 
▶Main work responsibilities:
 ‧Develop and promote information security and 
personal data strategies. 
 ‧Suggest information security and personal data 
policies and systems. 
 ‧Formulate to response material information security 
and personal data events and issues. 
 ‧Manage implementation plan and performance of 
information security and personal data. 
 ‧Responsible for planning, monitoring and executing 
information security and personal data management. 
 ‧Responsible for information security and personal 
data implementation.
Third level　Information security operation 
promotion
▶Information security management team: Members 
are represented by each respective system. 
▶Main work responsibilities: Responsible for 
information security and personal data policy 
promotion and communication.

Personal data protection
The Company introduces the personal information management system to consider the 
complete operation process of policyholder’s personal data collection, processing and 
utilization. In 2022, the Company passed the British Standard Institution BSI 10012: 2017 
Personal Information Management System (PIMS) certification, and conducted the "Personal 
Data Protection Law Advocacy Educational Training Course" at least once a year, to ensure 
that the data can be properly protected.
The protection and control mechanism of customer privacy can reduce the risk of leakage of 
customer data through network and e-mail personal data filtering and protection system and 
USB control mechanism. Through the Personal Data Management System (PIMS) certification, 
the introduction of personal data management system in all departments and branches, and 
workplace environment visit and education training in 50% of communication office, it shall 
strengthen the staff awareness of personal data protection; conduct the regular training of 
personal data security procedure drill; conduct the workplace environment visit activities, 
and strengthen the control mechanism of unsent emails, to reduce the risk of sensitive data 
leakage; conduct the regular inspection of mobile device application (APP) of the Company by 
third-party fair unit, and ensure the security of APP to reduce the risk of information security.

Complying with IFSR17
Participation in External Organization
To meet International Financial Reporting Standards 17 (IFRS 17) in 2026, the Company 
has set up an IFRS 17 steering committee, a project team and a dedicated team for the 
continuous cooperation with international experienced consultants and manufacturers to 
build and upgrade the IFRS17 related systems. The Company also continues to conduct 
various simulation trials and adjust the strategies of commodity, investment and risk control 
aspects to actively prepare for the integration. 
The progress of IFRS 17 project is described below:
Continuous optimizations for commodity, investment, risk control and other 
aspects:
On the commodity side, we will develop regular guaranteed commodities that 
meet the needs of customers and investment commodities targeted at silver 
and retired groups, and promote the commodity mix under investment principal 
contract and security collateral contract; continue to evaluate the impact of IFRS17 
on risk control related methods to make recommendations for modification; 
on investment side, coordinate with IFRS17 policy group to make a systematic 
adjustment on corresponding investment accounts. 
The Company actively participates in the external organizations, contributes and 
exchanges related experience, including The Life Insurance Association of the 
Republic of China, Life Insurance Management Institute of the Republic of China, 
Institute of Financial Law and Crime Prevention, Insurance Society of the Republic 
of China, Chinese Insurance Service Association, Taiwan Financial Services 
Roundtable, Risk Management Society of Taiwan, Pension Fund Association of the 
Republic of China, Monte Jade Science & Technology Association of Taiwan, Taiwan 
Insurance Institute, Taiwan Insurance Law Association, International Insurance 
Society, Actuarial Institute of the Republic of China, totally 13 institutes.
Project
Approach of the Company responding to IFRS 17
First stage
(2018~2019)
．IFRS 17 project team was established in 2018 and 
continues to work with international consultants
．	The first phase of the project will be completed by 
the end of 2019, focusing on educational training 
and initial financial impact assessment
Second stage 
(2020~2023)
．The main objective of the second phase of the project 
is to complete the establishment of data system, 
liability model and IFRS 17 related systems (including 
sub-ledger and general ledger), and to develop the 
company strategy
．	In 2021, the system supplier selection will be 
completed and the system requirement analysis will 
be started
．	The system construction will start in 2022, which is 
expected to be completed in the first quarter of 2023, 
with cross-system integration tests to be completed 
by the end of 2023 on schedule to ensure a smooth 
integration
2024
Enter into the parallel test phase and adjust 
according to the test situation
2025~2026
．	The account opening date is January 1, 2025, and 
the double-track accounting of IFRS4 & IFRS17 will 
be handled at the same time
．	It will be officially integrated in 2026

Mercuries Life Insurance believes that finance is the blood of 
sustainable economic development, and hopes to guide funds to 
sustainable development through the promotion of green finance. 
The Company follows the Principles for Responsible Investment (PRI), 
and takes the performance of investee companies in ESG into the 
investment reference. While pursuing financial stability and profit, 
the Company also actively exerts financial influence, and through 
digital transformation to achieve carbon reduction and social and 
environmental friendliness; In addition, the Company also adheres 
to the core value of "A word of promise, a friend for life" and actively 
cultivates a fair customer treatment service culture that covers the 
common prosperity of employees, subscribers and shareholders.

Responsible Investment
In accordance with the spirit of PRI responsible 
investment, when the Company conducts the 
standardized investment analysis and evaluation 
in the "Investment Policy" and "Institutional 
Investor Due Diligence Governance Policy", the 
environmental, social and corporate governance 
information of the investee company shall be 
incorporated into the investment reference basis.
According to the responsible investment principle 
of investment policy, the investment department 
has formulated the implementation principles of 
"environmental protection, social responsibility 
and corporate integrity" of relevant investment 
department and whether the target enterprise 
has implemented the anti-money laundering 
and counter terrorism financing. In the security 
investment and corporate lending process, 
whether the investee or credit enterprises conform 
to fulfill the principles of environmental protection, 
social sustainability and business integrity, and 
whether to implement the anti-money laundering 
and counter terrorism financing process, it shall 
understand the implementation in enterprise 
sustainability through the collection of ESG score 
and sustainability report or public information, 
while MSCI ESG grading, and negative tabulated list 
are revealed by the investee or credit enterprises 
in Bloomberg. The Company prohibits investment 
in the list of negative industries, and actively 
responds to the list of positive industries. After 
investment, the Company performs its responsible 
management obligations of investors by 
negotiating with enterprises and exercising voting 
rights. 
List of Positive/Negative Industries
List of positive tabulated industry/enterprise
Definition of positive tabulated industries: enterprises with good 
ESG performances. 
●List of positive tabulated economic activities
Types
Definitions
Renewable/
alternative energy
．Engaged in solar-related power generation, transmission and distribution
．Engaged in wind-related power generation, transmission and distribution

Negative Tabulated Industry

Definition of negative tabulated industries
．The object designated by the competent 
authority for sanctions in accordance with the 
Money Laundering Prevention Law and the 
Capital Terrorism Prevention Law. 
．Involved in material environmental violations, 
violations of human rights, labor rights, 
corporate governance or honest business 
operations, but no concrete improvement 
plan has been proposed. 
●List of negative tabulated industries
List of industries with high carbon emissions 
and high ESG risk
 ● List of industries with high carbon emissions
Types of 
Industry
Definitions
Arms and
ammunition
．Enterprises that manufacture or sell controversial weapons 
(mines, biological weapons, cluster munitions, depleted 
uranium, nuclear weapons, white phosphorus bombs, etc.)
．A vendor who illegally produces guns, mini weapons, 
ammunition, or illegally wholesales or retails in commercial 
markets
．Excluding enterprises specializing in defense, military and 
government markets
Cigarettes 
and tobacco
．All enterprises classified as tobacco producers, excluding 
distributors and retailers
．Engaged in the manufacture of tobacco products for 
absorption, chewing, containing or smelling from tobacco or 
tobacco substitutes
Gambling
．Engaged in non-public welfare lottery sales, or operating 
gaming fields, coin-operated gaming machines, gaming 
websites and other gaming services in violation of local laws 
and regulations
Porn
．Engaged in the business of running clubs, dance halls, 
restaurants, etc., accompanied by waiters
Drug
．Engaged in the production of psychotropic or narcotic drugs 
that sufficient to produce dependence for non-medical and 
scientific research purposes

Industry
Definitions
Petroleum, 
natural gas and 
coal products
．Engaged in oil and gas exploration, extraction, preliminary processing and 
preparation operations
．Separation and extraction of liquid hydrocarbons from hydrocarbons 
produced in shale oil or tar sands mining, oil or natural gas fields, and 
installation of oil rig
．Engaged in the business of converting crude oil and coal into usable 
products, including the separation of crude oil into fuel gas, gasoline, light 
oil, kerosene, diesel and other petroleum refining by cracking, distillation 
and other technologies
．Production of semi-coke, coke, coal tar and other products
．Manufacture of biogas/diesel

generation

facturing

cement, hydraulic cement, etc.

facturing
．Engaged in the smelting of ore for the production of pig iron, alloy iron and

direct reduced iron, scrap steel or cast ingot into carbon steel and alloy steel
．Engaged in making steel components by firing molten metal from pig iron, 
scrap iron and alloy raw materials into specific casting molds

Post-investment management
The Company shall hold the investment object during the holding period, and 
if the risks and opportunities related to the following ESG issues occur, it will, 
through telephone, email, interview, questionnaire, etc., understand the reasons 
and possible improvement practices, and review whether continuing to hold the 
investment object. 
1.Industries with high carbon emissions and high ESG risk that are defined by
the Company, and relevant management mechanisms and actions that are not 
specified in the sustainability report. 
2.There is no limit to the ESG risk level, and if the investment object has an issue 
of concern to the Company, involves significant ESG negative news or changes 
the nature of operations significantly to the extent that it may affect the ESG risk 
level. 
Investment Objectives of Investment Insurance 
Products Also Considered ESG Factor
The Company sold investment-linked insurance products, with connection to 
overseas funds, bonds, or ETF investment targets, also completed the revision 
of "Review Specifications for Recommendation of Investment Policy Connected 
Fund" and "Review Specifications for Recommendation of Investment Policy 
Connected Index Fund" in November 2021, and the ESG has been included 
in the investment target inspection standard, to implement the sustainable 
development, and to confirm whether the fund has incorporated ESG factors into 
the investment decision-making process, incorporated the local political and 
investment risks into the assessment, and excluded the investment in human 
rights disputes and arms and other related industries.

Inclusive Finance
Security Insurance Commodity 
Platform
As Taiwan estimates that it will enter a super-aged 
society from an elderly society in 2025, the retirement 
preparation is becoming more and more important to 
the public. The competent authority plans the retirement 
preparation platform combining the security, investment 
and promotion of public welfare. The Company actively 
responds to the government policies. The relevant website 
and product design of "Security Insurance Commodity 
Platform" was planned from 2021. As officially launched 
on July 1st, 2022, the platform will sell three kinds and six 
types of products, including the term life insurance, small-
amount life insurance for old age, and health insurance 
for major diseases, hoping to meet the basic retirement 
security needs of the public through simple and affordable 
insurance products.
Promotion of Microinsurance
Since 2014, it has vigorously promoted the microinsurance 
business, actively cooperated with colleges and universities, 
Children's Welfare Alliance, Association for Victims Support, 
Nantou County government and other schools, social 
welfare groups and local governments, and provided one-
year micro-injury insurance for economically disadvantaged 
groups and universities as well as colleges students whom 
are exempt from paying tuition and miscellaneous fees by 
donating insurance premiums, with the maximum amount 
of insurance per person up to NT$ 500,000, to help mitigate 
the financial impact of sudden accidents on families. 
Furthermore, it also helped to mitigate the financial impact 
of sudden accidents on families. From 2014 to now, a 
total of NT$ 29,158,572 of premiums have been donated, 
benefiting more than 110,000 insured people, including 
14,874 insured people in 2022; since 2017, microinsurance 
had been recognized by the FSC for six consecutive years, 
and was awarded the “Business Excellence Award” and “Care 
Award for Persons with Physical and Mental Disabilities” 
in 2022. In 2023, microinsurance premiums will continue 
The attendance rate of shareholders' meetings 
of listed companies in 2022 reached 98.55%
Sustainable Investment 
In response to the government's "5+2" investment in 
key innovative industries, the amount of sustainable 
investment in 2022 exceeded NT$54.58 billion, including 
biotechnology and medicine, green energy technology 
and environmental circular economy. In addition, we 
increase the proportion of sustainable investment every 
year to achieve the goal of strengthening green energy 
investment. In the life insurance industry, the sustainable 
investment initiatives to properly use the capital, not only 
promot the transformation of domestic industry, but also 
assist the development of green industry, to contribute to 
environmental sustainability.

Product Design to Meet a Variety of Needs—
Provide Multiple Insurances
Customer oriented products in 2022
The Elderly and Persons with Physical and Mental Disabilities
For the sake of benefiting the public, the Company launches the "J-Long-
Term Care Whole Life (JLTC)", and when a policyholder meets the status 
of long-term care, they can get compensation from such long-term care 
insurance, so as to arrange and enjoy proper care.
In addition, in order to meet the retirement planning needs of elderly 
customers, it also launches " TDL Interest Sensitivity Whole Life( Regular 
Payment ) (TDL)"," TYL Interest Sensitivity Whole Life( Regular Payment ) (TYL)" 
and " Single-Premium TFL Interest Sensitivity Whole Life ( Regular Payment 
) (TFL)" respectively for providing the dollar asset allocation planning for 
policyholders, accumulating wealth and rendering a whole life insurance 
guarantee at the same time, so as to meet the dual needs of the financial 
protection of policyholders and retirement planning.
Economically disadvantaged groups
For the purpose of reducing the pressure on those who are in the sandwich 
generation years with aging parents and young children, the " S - Dread 
Disease Benefit Insurance (A) (SDDB)" and the " SR - Dread Disease Benefit 
Insurance (A) (SRDDB)" are therefore introduced, which exchange low 
premiums for high protection and can be used as 
family subsidies during recuperating illness moment 
to avoid an income gap period.
In consideration of the protection needs of vulnerable 
groups in the event of accidental injury, the " 1 - Year 
Term GO - Accidental Dismemberment Insurance 
Rider (GODR)" is launched as a regular guaranteed 
commodity, with a premium adjusted with age and 
occupation level, and the insurance can be renewed 
up to 75 years old. This additional clause can be 
flexibly combined with life insurance, injury insurance, 
health insurance and other one-year ancillary 
insurances, perfectly suitable for small capital group 
or as a repurchase planning for policyholders who 
already have accident insurance.
To meet the needs of groups with limited budgets, 
“I-Small Amount Whole Life (ISAL)" is also introduced. 
It is simple to insure and can provide basic protection, 
with a premium is cheaper than that of ordinary whole 
life insurance, namely an amount from NT$ 100,000 to 
700,000 to enjoy a lifelong guarantee; furthermore, the 
" I- Small Amount Dismemberment Insurance Rider 
(ISPR)" launched with daily copperplate price in the 
same quarter is with more comprehensive protection; 
with respect to the needs of death or total disability 
protection, the " 5-Year X - Term Life (XRTL)" can 
meet the needs of different stages of life with small 
premium and large protection. 
Younger Group
Taking into account the health care needs of the 
young population, the “NSE-Hospital Indemnity 
Health Insurance (NSEHI)” has been introduced as 
policyholders are entitled to 1,000 times the daily 
amount of medical care during the contribution 
period and 3.3 times the total amount of premiums 
after the contribution period, so as to enjoy a peace of 
mind during the hospitalization, and without worrying 
about medical expenses.
As young groups may not be able to afford excessive 
premiums, the Company has launched " X - Term 
Life (XTL)", which has a small economic burden and 
can easily enjoy the basic security of life, and also 
launched " New S-Term Rider (NSTR)", which also 
enables the insured to enjoy high life insurance at 
a relatively affordable rate, and is suitable for the 
planning of petty bourgeoisie groups and family 
economic pillar. Particularly worth mentioning is the 
insurance is renewed, and will not be refused due to 
health problems.
In particular, in order to encourage young people 
to exercise more to build up their health, "IYC 
Catastrophic illness (IYC)" and " I-Long-Term Care 
Whole Life (ILTC)" are also introduced, in which the 
policyholder can upload the number of effective 
health steps in current policy year during the 
payment period, and if the discount standard is 
met, the discount will be provided, namely the 
renewal premium of next policy year (excluding other 
additional contracts and clauses) will be reduced. The 
premium feedback will increase with the accumulated 
effective health steps to encourage policyholders to 
develop a good habit of exercise.
Commuter population
Considering the injury risk of commuter groups, the “SF 
- Accidental Dismemberment  Insurance Rider (SFDR)" 
is specifically introduced. When policyholders are 
incapacitated from level 1 to 11 due to an "accidental 
injury accident", they will receive monthly support 
and be paid with "injury and disability insurance 
benefit” according to the degree of incapacitation, 
with the high cumulative number and maximum 
amount of payments. Mercuries Life Insurance 
provides policyholders with the assurance that they 
can rely on it if they have a mild disability. In addition, 
the " S-Accidental Fracture Reimbursement Insurance 
Rider (SFR)" is also launched at the same time to 
provide a fixed amount of fracture and dislocation 
surgery insurance benefits depending on fracture and

In addition, in view of the Company's " SP-Accidental Death & Dismemberment Insurance 
(SPA)", it also launches the exclusive" S-Accidental Medical Reimbursement Insurance 
Rider (SAMR)", which provides an actual payment of injury medical treatment within the
