In the pre-sales period, the Product Department of the Company shall provide the 
product-related information such as the document number, tariff and related numerical 
value, additional expense ratio, cost analysis, and term comparison table for the Marketing 
Department to make the marketing propaganda, and review whether the commodity 
rate, payment, example and relevant information of the marketing propaganda is 
correct according to the product marketing propaganda checklist provided by Marketing 
Department. The Company's product design process is in accordance with the relevant 
laws and regulations of the Insurance Law and is marked with warnings and cautions 
according to the laws.
An insurance contract is based on the principle of utmost good faith and is a contract in 
which the consideration is balanced between the proposer and the insurance company. 
Both the proposer and the insurance company shall fulfill the obligation of informing. 
When the business colleague enters into an insurance contract with the customer or 
the client makes an insurance demand, the Company shall ensure that the customer 
understands the insurance products purchased and its business as best as possible.
Business colleagues shall fully understand customers’ information, including their basic 
information, purposes and demands of insurance, motivations of insurance, whether their 
insurance conditions are met, their financial status, and sources of funds for insurance 
premium payment, and shall confirm that customers have understood the insurance 
products purchased, whether the insurance amounts and expenditures are equivalent 
to their actual demands; If purchasing foreign currency receipt and payment for non-
investment insurance products, shall confirm that the customer has understood the risk 
tolerance of foreign currency exchange rate; in case of purchasing investment insurance 
products, shall evaluate the investment attributes and risk tolerance, and make sure that 
the insured has truly understood that the investment gains and losses of the investment 
products purchased are borne by himself. 
In order to establish a corporate culture with “Fair Customer Treatment” as the core, we 
further established the fair customer treatment management meeting, held the cross-
department meeting on a quarterly basis, to jointly formulate the plans and measures to 
thoroughly implement the principle of fair customer treatment through this management 
meeting, and reported the meeting proposals to the Board of Directors, to ensure the 
implementation result, through the participation of the Board of Directors, and create a 
fair customer treatment culture from top to bottom.
In 2022, the external consultants lawyer were invited to conduct the advanced educational 
training on fair customer treatment, to understand the focus of competent authorities 
on the issues related to fair customer treatment. Through forum, the 
colleagues were invited to participate, to gradually guide the attention 
of various departments on this issue and their specific ideas based on 
the life cycle of insurance policies, as well as provide suggestions on fair 
customer treatment based on peer guidance experience.

Implement the Principle of Fair Customer 
Treatment from Four Major Aspects
Implementations in 2022
Aspects
Implementation of Financial Friendly 
Service

According to the “Guidelines for Financial Friendly Service of Insurance 
Industry”, we provide the place, communication and service, products and 
relevant information or statistical data to disabled people, allowing them 
to enjoy all basic rights as well as fair and reasonably convenient financial 
services. Form 2021, the insurance assistance mechanism and easy-to-
read version have been provided to cater to the needs of different types of 
persons with physical and mental disabilities.
Insurance for Physical and 
Mental Disabilities

In order to implement the principle of fair 
customer treatment and protect the insurance 
rights and interests of persons with physical and 
mental disabilities, the Company has formulated 
the "Operation Procedures and Notices for New 
Insurance Contract for Persons with Physical and 
Mental Disabilities", which includes the "Key Points 
for Examination and Evaluation of Insurance for 
Persons with Physical and Mental Disabilities" for 
the underwriters to follow. For persons with physical 
and mental disabilities, appropriate underwriting 
conditions shall be determined by referring to 
the underwriting assessment manual used by the 
Company during the underwriting review, and the 
insurance shall not be denied for no reason. Risk 
assessment and premium collection are also based 
on actuarial and statistical data as the basis of risk 
estimation. There is no unfair treatment for specific 
insured persons or just because the policyholder 
persons are physically and mentally disabled. The 
number of insured persons with physical and mental 
disabilities in 2022 increased by 0.09% compared to 
the previous year.
Prevention of Financial 
Exploitation of Senior Citizens

In order to strengthen and protect the consumer rights 
of elderly policyholders, we adjusted the content of the 
sales structure of investment products to be divided 
into "products that can be sold to customers aged 
65 and above" and "products that can be insured up 
to 64 years old" to ensure the suitability of products 
for elderly insured customers in 2022. For elderly 
customers applying for termination of the contract, 
partial withdrawal, preservation of policy loan, or when 
customers over 65 years old themselves acting as 
insurance premium payers, special personnel will be 
designated to remind such customers of the potential 
impact of product characteristics on them and various 
adverse factors, relevant rights and risks, so as to 
safeguard the rights and interests of policyholders. 
Furthermore, when applying for automatic transfer or 
credit card authorization of agreed or changed renewal 
insurance premium, and if the authorized person is 
aged 65 or above as an informal policyholder or the 
insured, the "authorized person" shall be recorded 
by telephone or visited in person to confirm that the 
elderly customer is aware of the change and can afford 
the insurance cost.

Policyholder Service Preferential 
Measures for Disaster Affected 
Individuals

After suffering from 918 Strong Earthquake, Super 
Typhoon Hinnamnor, etc. in 2022, we immediately 
searched whether the affected people were our 
policyholders, and immediately activated the policyholder 
care and assistance through our regional customer service 
and agency force. We also published the policyholder care 
measures on our official website and press release. If the 
affected people are our policyholders, they can apply for 
special service measures as follows:
1. Policy loan interest deduction
2. Free replacement of policy
3. Deferred payment for renewal premiums
4. Fast settlement
5. Deferred payment for principal of housing loan
Friendly Service Locations

All the service counters of the Company provide the 
special guidance services for the disabled and visually 
impaired groups, 100% of them are equipped with barrier 
free ramps, and about 70% have the disabled toilets, 
providing the most thoughtful services for the people 
with inconvenient movement and creating friendly 
service environment for all the policyholders. In addition, 
we set up accessible space in most of the cooperative 
bancassurance channels. Considering the transportation 
inconvenience of people at Hualien, Taitung and offshore 
island areas, 4 agency offices and 110 cooperative 
financial access service sites (as of December 2022) have 
been established there to facilitate the people in remote 
areas. We also promote the anti-money laundering and 
other related initiatives in the training of personnel from 
cooperative bancassurance channel, totally about 13 
hours.
Most cooperative bancassurance channels have set up 
barrier-free facilities and friendly services for persons with 
physical and mental disabilities, such as accessible service 
counter, service bell, reading glasses for the elderly and 
ATM accessible on wheelchairs.
When the bancassurance customers handle the contract 
change, if the signature style doesn't agree with the 
original style, and it is not convenient for customers to go 
to the service centers of the Company in person to handle 
the contract change, the auxiliary training staff of the 
department will adopt the visiting service and confirm the 
customer's identity to help handle the contract change.
Care Measures for COVID-19 
Affected Policyholder

In 2022, the policyholder service and care measures in 
response to COVID-19 in 2021 was continued to ensure 
the health of employees and the rights and interests of 
policyholders; for insured households affected by the 
epidemic, services such as deferred payment of insurance 
premiums for renewal, single window preservation 
service, preferential measures for policy borrowing, loan 
programs for insurance policies to assist economically 
vulnerable households and leniency in claims settlement 
were also provided to reduce impact of the epidemic 
and help insured households tide 
over difficulties. In addition, from 
the standpoint of social justice 
and benefiting policyholders, the 
interim claim settlement measures in 
response to the COVID-19 outbreak 
was extended until December 19, 2022.
In 2021, the "Preferential Loan Rate Project 
of Bailout Policy for Economic Vulnerable 
Group” was launched to assist 8,588 
policyholders,10,257 policies with a total 
borrowing amount of NT$732 million, 
receiving the "Bailout Excellence Award" from 
the FSC.
In 2022, continued to handle the "Preferential 
Loan Rate Project of Bailout Policy for 
Economic Vulnerable Group" to help the 
policyholders in economic difficulties tide over 
difficulties by extending the application period 
for 6 months. By the end of December 2022, 
the total number of applications was 167 
/194 cases, and the total loan amount was 
NT$ 13,841,877. 
Listen to Customers’ Feedback
Mercuries Life Insurance values the feedbacks of each customer 
and follows the fair customer treatment principle to protect 
customers, and also provides the caring services and most suitable 
solutions to customers. The customer service center is located in 
the headquarters. 
In order to confirm the customers' feelings and ensure the service 
quality, the Company conducts a satisfaction survey from the 
aspects of customer service staff's clarity of speech, explanation 
content and service attitude through random sampling. The 
average satisfaction survey in 2022 was 99.29%, 0.20% higher than 
that in 2021.

Satisfaction Survey of Policyholder

The Company attaches great importance to the customers' feelings and experiences. In 
order to listen to customers' voices to provide more perfect service, at the beginning of 
2021, we entrusted the impartial third-party survey company to conduct the customer 
satisfaction survey again. Through the collection, analysis and understanding of customer 
ideas and opinions, we are committed to deepening the customer experience and 
improving the service quality and efficiency, and promoting customer satisfaction. The 
results of the survey shall be the reference to improve the Company's service quality, 
and make improvements and decide the optimization direction according to the analysis 
results.
In 2022, focusing on the after-sales service, the survey list excluded the customer of a new 
policy. Among the service performance of the Company, the agency satisfaction must be 
the highest, namely quickly response to deal with the needs, have enough professional 
knowledge with warm service attitude, and be professional as the most important 
advantages; the highest satisfaction of internal staff is cordial and enthusiastic service 
attitude, sufficient professional knowledge, complete and correct information and clear 
reply to customer questions; the highest satisfaction of the customer service center is 
the cordial and enthusiastic service attitude; the highest satisfaction of the policyholder 
zone on the official website is high stability and not easy to crash; the highest satisfaction 
of policyholder APP is that the information provided is simple and easy to understand. 
Through customer satisfaction survey to master the evaluation of the Company, track and 
understand customer opinions and feedback, improve the quality of various services, so 
as to provide customers with more satisfactory services. 
Promote Customer Experience Service Plan

In order to deepen the customer experience and establish a customer-centered service 
culture, a code of conduct for service is set up to be followed to improve the service 
quality. To fulfill the commitment of customer service training based on the principle of 
fair customer treatment, customer experience service optimization and counseling, a 3-year 
customer service training service blueprint has been formulated.
In 2022, the Company cooperated with consultants and lecturers to launch the "Training 
Course for Customer Service Supervisor", and the branch company then assigns 
supervisors or senior colleagues to participate in the "seed training" of customer service. 
Through the establishment of the concept of "Mystery Customer" and the existing 
customer service training materials, the Company has introduced the concept of service 
supervision for its branch to establish a service supervision process and maintain service 
quality. 
Smooth Complaint Channel

Mercuries Life Insurance deeply roots its service concept in the hearts of all employees and 
accepts different voices and opinions humbly. In order to meet the needs of all parties, we 
provide multiple channels such as written, telephone and the Internet to establish perfect 
customer complaint handling procedures, hold management meetings every quarter to 
make the state analysis report and provide suggestions for review and improvement, to 
avoid the recurrence of dispute cases.
Complaint case management meeting is held every held quarter, and the focus of 
the meeting is not to discuss the case, but for the complaint case analysis, review, 
improvement measures, and statistical analysis and description of the case state, hoping 
to avoid the occurrence of complaint case from the source.
Improvements in Negative Events

Policyholders' phone reactions and suggestions are sorted out and 
analyzed every month and provided for inspection by relevant units. In 
2022, a total of 5,066 calls and complaints were received, which were all 
handled by customer service staff. In the future, project process reviews 
will be carried out to improve customer experience.

The "Life Transfer Station" TAB has been added to the Mobile 
Office APP, which enables the customers to understand the 
necessary stages of life and the risks they may encounter 
through the APP. Based on interactive experience, the 
customers can choose the risks they care about, and the 
system can tailor the insurance products that are most 
suitable for customers at this stage. At present, the APP 
has completed the part of recommending the security 
products, which has been opened for agency force to lead 
the customers to use, and will be optimized after collecting 
feedback. In addition, the APP will continue to develop 
the function of linking the mobile insurance, optimize the 
insurance process, and let the customers experience the 
one-stop insurance experience. It is expected to continue 
to develop the product recommendation function for 
investment products and profit variation products in 2023. 
Moreover, through the advanced big data and AI prediction 
technology, we shall actively develop the "Customer Rescue" 
customer recommendation system, provide the high-quality 
customer recommendation list, accurately predict and 
real-time meet the customer security needs, improve the 
customer transaction probability, greatly reduce the agent's 
marketing visit time, and quickly improve the marketing 
performance.
Online Insurance Purchasing

In response to the COVID-19 outbreak, to enable the agency 
force to successfully serve the customers and promote 
the business while reducing the risk of direct contact with 
customers, we launched the online insurance purchasing by 
"insurance paper documents, taking photos to send back, 
confirmation through video". Subsequently, we actively 
developed the "mobile online insurance service system". 
Agency force can directly send back the relevant electronic 
documents through the system to assist the customers to 
complete the insurance purchasing. In order to promote 
the convenience of business tools and business processing 
efficiency, there newly added the "new contract mobile reply 
operation", so that the agency force can check all kinds of 
new contract underwriting related notes in real time and 
upload the online reply directly through iPad, which not 
only can reduce the paper work to carry out the energy 
conservation and carbon reduction, but also can increase 
the efficiency of the underwriting cases, and shorten the 
process time.
Fast and Convenient Service
Mobile Service
The Company's mobile service includes the mobile 
insurance purchasing, premium payment, claim settlement, 
policyholder service, and other comprehensive services. 
The agents only needs iPad and mobile service statement 
as well as confirmation sheet to assist the policyholder and 
potential policyholder to complete the insurance purchasing, 
claim settlement or contract change and other services.
Online Insurance Service
Number of online insured persons:
New contract data
Mobile Insurance Service
To simplify the application and handling process for 
policyholders and respond to and implement the energy 
savings and carbon reduction, we launched the "Mobile 
Insurance Service" function in April 2016, which has three 
major functions: electronic writing, automatic verification 
and real-time notification. Agency force can assist the 
policyholders in performing policy changes through iPad 
at any time and any place. There are only three simple 
steps: input, confirm, check and upload, and then ask 
the policyholder to sign a written statement to complete 
the application of contract content change or remittance 
account agreed in the insurance policy. Contract change 
is simplified as the policyholder only needs to sign a 
written statement, the cover of account passbook can be 
photographed and uploaded, and the agency force do not 
need to carry all kinds of complicated paper application 
forms, so the application for contract 
change can be easily completed. Once 
uploaded, the data is fully protected by 
information security system and we will 
send a message to the policyholder to 
confirm the successful data upload.

Insurance/Claim Blockchain Services

In order to improve the efficiency and facilitate the service, the Company 
cooperates with the Life Insurance Association to make use of the safe and 
convenient blockchain technology in 2021, so that the policyholder can access 
the “Mobile Insurance Service/Mobile Claims” through agency force, and transfer 
the basic data change or claim application to the cooperative insurance company 
through the Consortium Blockchain mechanism, so as to avoid the inconvenient 
documents circulation among several insurance companies. In December 2022, 
"Mobile Claims" joins the "Digital Identity Verification" pilot program, which 
combines insured identity confirmation, paper and electronic declaration signing 
to improve the convenience of claims settlement services. By the end of 2022, 
the utilization rate of the alliance chain or Medical Union increased by 65.34% 
compared with the previous year. 
Mercuries Life Insurance APP and Online Service

IIn 2021, in order to facilitate customers to quickly find our APP in mobile 
application system providers, our mobile APP was renamed as “Mercuries Life 
Insurance APP”. The Company also launched the “Quick Login” service, which 
enables the users to quickly log in with biometric or graphic identification of 
mobile devices through account number and password agreement, to increase 
the convenience of use of policyholder and improve the customer experience.
As the number of automated trading services increases year by year, by the end of 
2022, the proportion of changes in policy data, policy loans, or investment-related 
policy objectives and transactions through policyholder online section accounting 
for the total number of transactions was as shown in the table below. It can be 
seen that online trading volume is growing year by year. 60% of the policyholders 
are used to conducting the transactions online, with the online application rate 
of "policy loan" and "fund transaction" approaching or exceeding 70%. Our 
automated services enable the policyholders to communicate with us when they 
want and in the way they want. Consistent with the policyholder experience, the 
using ratio has increased year by year, and we have fulfilled our promise to provide 
the policyholder with diverse service channels.

2022 Goals and Achievements
 Promoted the "Talent DNA- Leadership Management Assessment", laid out all levels of management and understood 
the status of reserve talents at all levels.
Expanded the succession plan, and strengthened the executive leadership course; 60~70 junior-senior executives
participated in the program and we aim to cultivate the successors with potential and development capability.
 The total investment in internal staff training cost exceeded NT$ 7.31 MILLION, and the total training hours exceeded 
50,000 HOURS, with average training hours of 28.51 HOURS per person.
 The total investment of agency force training cost exceeded NT$ 23.45 MILLION, and the total training hours 
exceeded 350,676 HOURS, with an average training hours of 36.52 HOURS per person.
 The pass rate of new staff to obtain the personal insurance agent license was 68.5%, better than the industry average 
of 39.6%. At the same time, in 2022, there were 9,129 agents qualified for selling the investment-type products (the 
pass rate of the test was 79.3%, better than the industry average of 43%), and 8,773 agents qualified for selling the 
foreign-currency non-investment products (the pass rate of the test was 76.6%, better than the industry average of 
49.2%).

Appendix
Starting Salary

Mercuries Life Insurance offers the salary superior to market standard, which is 
competitive externally and fair internally, regardless of gender and age. In 2022, 
our starting salary was NT$ 34,900, 1.09 times higher than the market freshman 
starting salary of NT$ 32,000 (salary survey statistical result for occupational 
category in July 2021 from the Ministry of Labor), and 1.3 times higher than the 
basic wage of NT$32,000 announced by the Executive Yuan. In addition, for the 
full-time internal employees of non-supervisory positions in 2022, the average 
annual salary was NT$ 944,000. And we have consecutively raised our employee 
salaries for 11 years, with an average increase of 3.0% in 2022. Through the 
salary system, we expect to encourage the employees to contribute their efforts 
and to have full driving power and confidence in their career development.
Note: The starting salary of the Companys grassroots employees (including training students) is 
NT$ 26,400, which is in line with the basic salary.
Welfare System

The Company has formulated the Employee Welfare Committee Method, providing not 
only business trip allowance, preferential housing loan, holiday gifts, maternity leave, 
employee insurance or bonus, incentive travel and employee preferred shares for internal 
employees, but also professional examination incentive system, club activities, employee 
marriage and maternity subsidy, travel allowance, annual health examination, and group 
insurance coverage, staff MRT station shuttle bus, etc. Moreover, an annual tourism 
allowance of NT$ 6,500 will be provided to employees who have been on the job for one 
year, to encourage the balanced development of both body and mind.

Appendix
Reassured Labor Pension Plan

No matter in the new or old system of employee retirement, we provide the retirement 
fund in full and pension superior to the requirements specified in the regulations, thereby 
assuring that the employees have sufficient living guarantee after retirement. We provide 
the retirement severance fund superior to the regulations to employees adopting the old 
system of service years. For employees retiring and satisfying the retirement qualification, 
the upper limit of severance pay is calculated based on the 55 cardinal numbers specified 
in the regulations as the retirement fund(The agency business supervisor is limited to 
a maximum of 66 bases). For the employees retiring but do not meet the retirement 
qualifications, the severance pay is issued according to the calculation of service year.
Performance Evaluation

Each year, we establish the annual performance goal together with employees according 
to the annual business plan, and also classify into three stages the establishment of goal 
at the beginning of the year, mid-term goal execution status tracking, and year-end goal 
review. In addition, the measures of year-end bonus and annual salary adjustment are 
linked to the annual performance evaluation result. Furthermore, for the employees with 
poor performance, we also assist them to adopt the performance improvement guidance, 
periodically track and discuss the employee working conditions. Related department and 
related division KPIs include ESG-related indexes, which serve as an important reference 
for annual performance evaluation and are linked to the salary. In 2022, all Mercuries Life 
Insurance employees participated in the annual performance review.

professional training according to the job ranks and course objectives, so 
as to improve the occupational competitiveness of employees, cultivate the 
professional management talents, and implement sustainable business. 
Furthermore, we encourage the employees to obtain the US license of Life Office 
Management Association (LOMA) and relevant professional licenses for the work 
fields, and provide the welfare of examination subsidy. We build a digital learning 
platform to provide the employees, so as to improve the convenience and 
accessibility of learning. We also provide the diverse training plans with depth and 
breadth, so that employees can grow together with the enterprise. In 2022, we 
invested a total exceeding NT$ 7.31 million training expense, and the total training 
hours of internal employee exceeded 50,000 hours, with an average training hour 
per capita of 28.51 hours.

Succession Plan

To cultivate and continuously track the talents with high potential, 
we have activated the “Succession Plan” in 2019 and selected 60-70 
intermediate and senior supervisors to participate in the plan in 2022. 
Through the stages of talent selection, cultivation and development, 
evaluation and review, we aim to cultivate the successors with 
potential and development capability, thereby reducing the 
deficiency in the key management talents in the Company and 
allowing both the Company and employees to head toward the goal 
of sustainable business together.
Encourage employees to 
participate in the community

To encourage staff to participate in volunteer activities, 
they may participate in volunteer activities organized 
by public welfare organizations such as government 
agencies, people's organizations approved by the 
Ministry of the Interior and funds approved by 
competent authorities.0.5 days of volunteer leave 
will be applied for if more than 3 hours of volunteer 
activities are accumulated; and after 6 hours, you can 
take one day off. You can apply for up to 2 days a year. 
In 2022, 69 people participated in volunteer activities 
and applied for 119 volunteer leave days.
Promote a business talent 
cultivation program

In order to enable outstanding young partners to 
enter the door of life insurance and grow steadily 
without worries, Mercuries Life Insurance launches 
the “Reserve Account Ssupervisor(AS) Program” and 
“Junior Manager Training Program” for a total of 27 
months. It is expected to help and urge business 
personnel to grow rapidly through project training, 
so that business executives can achieve win-win-
win results in personal performance, personnel 
cultivation and organizational development.

Appendix
▶Three training processes, to set goals and
directionThree training processes of “Base”, “Root” 
and “Promotion”

Mercuries Life Insurance has established a comprehensive personnel training system, and 
in order to help new employees set clear goals and directions at the beginning of their life 
insurance career, Mercuries Life Insurance has also divided training into three categories: 
“Base”, “Root” and “Promotion” from the guidance of field new personnel to obtain 
professional certificates, and training of sales and recruitment skills, and then develop a 
grand life insurance career view.
In 2022, 647 new colleagues were instructed to obtain the license of the life insurance 
agent, with a passing rate of 68.5%, better than the industry average of 39.6%. At the same 
time, in 2022, there are 9,129 agents qualified for selling investment-type products (the 
pass rate of the test is 79.3%, better than the industry average of 43.0%), and 8,773 agents 
qualified for selling the foreign-currency non-investment products (the pass rate of the 
test is 76.6%, better than the industry average of 49.2%), accounting for 85.9% and 82.55% 
of the total number of agents respectively, showing the positive growth for six consecutive 
years.
◎Basic Training
The first and most important step in the life insurance career is to obtain a 
professional license. To this end, we provide certification training courses 
through regional training units on a regular basis to assist colleagues in their 
professional knowledge. We also compile teaching materials for certification 
qualification tests to assist colleagues in obtaining certification. In addition, in 
order to help new agents quickly understand the Company's various products 
and sales laws and regulations, regular commodity classes are set up to 
help colleagues become more professional with high-quality life insurance 
business.
◆	 Related courses: trade union class, foreign currency insurance commodity license 
class, investment insurance commodity license class, commodity class, etc.
◎Rooted Training
The professionalism of the business staff is an indicator of Mercuries Life 
Insurance's professional image. In addition to marketing, the client service 
can not be ignored. To this end, we strengthen the professional competence 
of our business staff through two courses: rooted training and on-the-job 
administrative training. Moreover, the life insurance consultant examination 
is held regularly to check whether the business personnel understand the 
Company's commodity terms, various administrative procedures and relevant 
laws and regulations, so as to strictly check the professional image of the 
Company.
◆	 Related courses: On-the-job training of administrative operations (elementary/
advanced), rooted training of agents, etc.

Launch the new digital learning 
platform of "Mercuries Digital 
College"

The new digital learning platform of "Mercuries 
Digital College" was officially launched on January 
1, 2021. It has convenience, openness, timelessness 
and customized function, with a more intuitive and 
convenient user interface and more diversified digital 
content planning, and hardware equipment that can 
accommodate more users at the same time. In 2022, 
a total of 450 online courses in eight categories were 
opened, which increased by 85 compared with 2021 
through actively expanding the learning breadth, and 
striving to improve the professional functions and 
soft strength of agents. Diversified courses covered 
information security, money laundering prevention, 
business quality, friendly aged and vulnerable groups, 
tax-related, investment and finance, current news 
analysis, product introduction, sales and recruitment 
courses, and a total of 310,762 people were registered 
for training. In addition, through written and on-
site review by the Life Insurance Association, a 
6-hour external common law compliance course was 
permitted on its platform.

◎Promotion Training
With the promotion of position, business personnel should have their 
own growth goals at each stage. Business specialists should focus on the 
development of good habits and sales skills, business executives must be 
familiar with how to promote the life insurance business, and develop a good 
concept and attitude to increase the number of employees. To this end, we 
arrange promotion training for our business staff at the beginning of each 
stage of their promotion to develop more efficient management attitudes 
and methods, not only through re-examining themselves through the course 
content, but also through mutual discussion among colleagues of the same 
rank.
◆	 Related courses: Account Supervisor promotion training, business assistant 
manager promotion training, business manager promotion training, middle 
and senior manager promotion training, office manager promotion training, etc

MOD educational training platform
We cooperate with Chunghwa Telecom to build an internal MOD educational training platform, entrust 
Chunghwa Telecom to set up the viewing equipment in all locations of the Company in Taiwan, and 
have invested a lot of education and training expenses in the headquarters to build a special studio, 
purchase more equipment related to photography and editing, and recruit the talents related to 
communication media. One episode of the MOD morning meeting educational training program is 
created weekly, totally 338 episodes by the end of 2022. The average broadcasting rate has achieved 
above 80%. MOD morning meeting educational training is committed to deepening the content of the 
program. In 2022, through the establishment of network questionnaire survey and communication with 
business units, it is expected to improve the participation of agents, condense the centripetal force, and 
improve the incentive effect.
In 2022, the annual total investment amount exceeds NT$ 22.45 million, and 
the total training hours of agency force exceeds 350,676 hours, with the average 
training hour of about 36.52 hours per capita.

Mercuries Life Insurance have established 
the “Human Rights Policy” based on the 
approval of the Board of Directors in 
2019 and in accordance with the human 
rights protection spirit and basic principle 
specified in the international human 
rights conventions, such as “Universal 
Declaration of Human Rights”, “The United 
Nations Global Compact”, “International 
Labor Convention” and “Declaration 
on Fundamental Principles and Rights 
at Work”, to provide diverse and equal 
employment opportunities regardless 
of differences in gender, race, language, 
thought, religion, age, marriage status, 
and appearance, etc., so as to create a 
health and safe working environment. 
Furthermore, we have also employed 21 
professional visually impaired massage 
therapists and provided the disabled rights 
and convention compliance promotional 
courses for employees, to increase the 
employees’ understanding on the rights 
of the disabled, thereby promoting the 
equality of working environment.
Parental Leave Table
To enable staff to make major career 
plans at ease, provide full support to their 
childcare and related planning needs, we 
encourage the employees to apply for 
maternity leave or child care in accordance 
with the law, so that they can take care of 
their family and work at the same time.

Mercuries Life Insurance provides multiple channels to receive comments from employees, 
responds to their proposals in a positive and attentive manner in order to improve the 
occupational environment and labor-management relationship. For internal staff, the Company 
regularly issues the internal staff electronic report every month and sets up the staff browsing 
and discussion section; the agency force can interact with the Company through the publications 
such as Fengxiang Monthly and electronic systems, to ensure the smooth communication 
between the Company and staff.
Sexual Harassment Prevention / General Complaint 
e-mail Address
Internal employee: Human Resources Department, Ms. Hsieh, 02-2345-5511 ext.22200
Complaint e-mail address:hr_01@mail.mli.com.tw, which has dedicated personnel to receive the 
whistle blowing cases, complaints and recommendations from employees in order to provide the 
channels and to protect the rights of employees to file complaints.
Agency force: Please contact each region’s agent service section
Periodically Convene the Labor-Management Meeting
The Company convenes the labor-management meeting quarterly, in which the Company policy 
is promoted, and the Company's business current status is explained. The ratio of attending labor 
and management representatives is close to 1:1 as a periodic communication mechanism for 
internal employees, and the labor representatives are able to provide recommendations directly 
in the meeting, thereby allowing the Company to understand the needs of employees and 
improve the working environment timely. Four meetings were held in 2022 to discuss the issues 
related to employee welfare ,the group agreement covers 100% of all employees.
Agent Communication Channel
The Company values the feedbacks of each agent, holds irregular convention of senior officers’ 
meetings, product consultation meetings, investment-linked product consultation meetings, 
and district agency managers meetings, etc., to communicate the sales topics with agency force 
in different job ranks. Furthermore, we also provide the agent proposal submission mechanism, 
and the first line of agents can provide the improvement recommendations on the current 
operation of the Company, which will be replied after evaluated by relevant departments. In 
2022, there were 115 cases successfully, to listen to the advice of agents, and create an effective 
response mechanism for agent proposal.

Appendix
Safety and Health Management
Mercuries Life Insurance attaches importance to the workplace safety and health, 
invested over NT$ 4.1 million in 2022 to improve the workplace safety and health and 
promote various improvement measures.
The Company establishes an occupational safety and health management plan every year 
and implements, reviews and improves relevant safety and health matters according to 
the plan. In addition, the Company has formulated the safety and health work rules, which 
are announced to employees to know and abide by. The occupational safety and health 
committee meetings are held quarterly to collect opinions from employees for discussion 
and improvement, and to discuss the safety and health issues of the Company by 
committee members, and evaluate whether there are improvement items, improvement 
methods and improvement results.
The Company belongs to the Type III Workplace, where there is almost no high-risk 
operation. The air quality of the office environment is monitored in accordance with 
occupational safety and health laws. The office lamps are bright and have sufficient 
illumination. Every day there are cleaning staff to tidy up the workplace; and no 
biochemical noise pollution and other hazard factors.
The office building and policyholder service counter locations of the Company are 
installed with AED “Automated External Defibrillator”, barrier-free facilities, and security 
personnel to ensure the safety of employees. In addition, the human resource department 
and communication offices in each area and regional attendance records, it could indicate 
the proper statistical occurrence of occupational disasters, in light of improving the 
success rate of precious rescue timing via complete prevention and preparation works.

Appendix
Employee Health Services
Health service
Measure
Employee health 
guidance and 
promotion
The Company employs the dedicated labor health service staff to provide the staff health guidance and promotion services, and provide the free 
registration for face-to-face consultations with on-site specialists; the nurses will make an appointment with computer room shift colleagues, drivers, 
middle-aged and elderly employees, pregnant and female colleagues within one year after delivery, as the priority consultation objects according to 
the schedule. We also open the chance for our staff to sign up for face-to-face health and physical and psychological consultation. All staff with high 
risk after assessment will be tracked down as care or improvement targets.
Maternal health 
protection
Maternal health protection measures will be provided to all internal staff of the Company. The object is the staff during pregnancy or within one year 
after delivery, with one bottle of fresh milk or soybean milk per week. The number of beneficiaries was 36 persons in 2022. And we also set up breast 
milk collecting (feeding) room for the use of employees in need.
Safety and health 
advocacy
The Company configured occupational safety and health management personnel and labor health service personnel shall regularly advocate 
the information related to health and safety, and invite the on-site specialist or external professional lecturer to provide the special lectures for 
employees to participate in, and pass the health knowledge in e-paper regularly.
Employee 
assistance plan 
(EAP)
We have cooperated with the Employee Assistance Program Service Center of Hsinchu City to provide the unlimited hours and number of times of 
telephone consultation services to employees for psychological counseling served by psychologists and consultants with professional knowledge 
backgrounds. In 2022, the employee assistance plan Phase I telephone consultation was used 65 person-times, Phase II face-to-face consultation was 
used 28 person-times, and the investment amount was NT$ 261,200.
Healthcare room
ltThe Company has set up the healthcare room, providing simple wound dressing articles, facial masks, height and weight measuring devices, and
blood pressure meters for staff to use at any time, and to understand their basic physical condition.

Employee Occupational Disaster Events, Number of Days of Loss, and Absence Table
Note:
(1) Injury ratio calculation formula: Injury ratio (IR) = (Number of people injured / Total number of 
       working hours) x 200,000
(2) There are no cases of occupational diseases in 2022
(3) Loss of working hours ratio calculation formula: Loss of working hours ratio (LDR) = (Total number of 
       days lost due to injury / Total number of working hours) x 200,000
(4) Absence rate (AR) = Number of days of absence due to sick leave and occupational injury / Total        
       number of working days × 100%
(5) In this table, the definitions adopted for the calculation standards of the injury ratio and loss of 
       working hours ratio are higher than the definitions specified by the Ministry of Labor of Taiwan, and 
       the calculation starts from the next day of the occurrence of accident, and all injuries related to work, 
       regardless of the severity of injuries, are included in the calculation.
(6) Occupational accidents during the commute refer to the traffic accident.

Academic Donation 
As an insurance company, we have been committed to 
financial insurance education for a long time, and cultivate 
campus elites. In addition to sponsoring the Risk and 
Insurance Research Center of National Chengchi University 
to engage in insurance academic development for 9 
consecutive years, and sponsoring the Financial Technology 
Industry and Academic Cooperation Alliance (now is the 
Scientific Research Industrialization Platform of National 
Chengchi University)to support the FinTech innovation for 
5 consecutive years, we also continue to cooperate with 
the RMIM Inc. in the donation of RMIM health and finance 
magazines for 8 consecutive years. We also strongly support 
the holding of insurance related seminars, Such as 2022 
East Asia and Pacific Insurance Forum, etc.
Campus Internship
By providing internship programs for college students, 
we cooperate with insurance, finance and other related 
departments to conduct academic and practical exchanges, 
reduce the gap between learning and practice, promote 
the connection between students and practical work, and 
further retain the talents for the Company. The Company 
cooperates with 8 universities and 9 departments, such 
as the Department of Finance of I-Shou University, the 
Department of Insurance of Chaoyang University of 
Technology, the Department of Risk Management and 
Insurance of Shih Chien University, the Department of 
Finance of National Chung Hsing University, the Department 
of Financial Management of Kun Shan University, the 
Department of Finance and Department of Senior Services 
Industry Management of Minghsin University of Science 
and Technology, and provides a total of 109 students to 
enter the Company for the internship, and understand the 
operation of the insurance company.

Cultivate the Sports Atmosphere among Citizens
Focusing on the "health risk" orientation of Taiwanese, it shall promote the development 
of sports culture of the citizens through long-term promotion of sports activities, so as to 
cultivate the strong body and enhance the awareness of health risk management. Mercuries 
Life Insurance has long supported the development of domestic sports for a long time and 
participated in various sports event promotion over a decade, in light of expanding the 
sports atmosphere to all villages and townships domestically. In 2022, our contribution in 
the sports events reached NT$ 35.84 million, and the number of people benefited exceeded 
97,000. Through participation in sports games, we look forward to establishing health risk 
awareness and creating the culture of sports for all citizens.
Up to the year of 2022, Mercuries Life Insurance has received the award of “Golden Prize” 
in the sponsorship category of the “Sports Activist Awards” from the Sports Administration, 
Ministry of Education for 14 consecutive years, showing that Mercuries Life Insurance is 
an important promoter of domestic sports. In 2022, we took practical actions to support 
"Mercuries Taiwan Masters Invitational Golf Tournament” and won the “Bronze Award” in 
promotion category.
A m o n g  t h e m ,  t h e  " Ya t e 
Cup Intellectual Disability 
Games" protects the students 
with physical and mental 
disabilities with insurance. 
Through participating in sports 
activities, the students can 
enhance their learning ability, 
improve their confidence, 
and better integrate into the 
community.
 
 ◆  Sponsored Taiwan Master and Mercuries Golf Invitational 
Tournament 
Organized by Mercuries Enterprises, the “Mercuries Taiwan Masters Invitational Golf 
Tournament” is the only professional men's golf tournament in Taiwan that has been 
organized by a single company for more than 30 years. It is also the first international event 
in Taiwan to be included in the Asian Golf Tour. In 2022, a total of 126 domestic professionals 
and amateurs will be attracted to compete.
 ◆  Organized Mercuries Life Insurance Cup Teeball National 
Tournament
We have promoted Teeball for primary school students for 13 consecutive years. In 2022, 
91 teams and 1,365 players participated. For 13 years in total, 1,025 teams and more than 
15,000 players have participated in the Tournament.

◆ Sponsored Mercuries Cup Charity Road Running
Sponsored for 16 consecutive years, in 2022, "Love‧All Over" was the focus of activity 
planning, to support national sports and donate to visual-impaired disabilities groups, we 
actively called on all the colleagues of the agency force to participate in the charity activity 
and road running together, and set up the booths on the scene to enjoy running with the 
public, attracting more than 2,000 runners to enjoy running together.
◆  Sponsored various sports activities in secondary schools
The Taiwan High Secondary School Sports Association was committed to promoting sports 
competition and enhancing the relationship between schools. It organized secondary 
school sports activities including: High School Basketball League (HBL), High School 
Volleyball League (HVL), Junior High School Basketball League (JHBL), Junior High School 
Volleyball League (JHVL), High School Football League (HFL), Women's Softball League, 
Hot Dance Competition, etc. Mercuries Life Insurance had sponsored all secondary 
school sports events for 14 consecutive years, and its executives not only attended press 
conferences every year, but also encouraged the winners by presenting the Rebound King/
Rebound Winner award at the HBL final awards ceremony. In addition, Mercuries Life 
Insurance’s mascot Boby also performed a wonderful cheerleading performance in halftime 
with professional dancers at the HBL final to cheer on all the players and support the 
development of campus sports with practical actions.
Children Development Care
Children are the seeds of hope for the future. To this end, Mercuries Life Insurance has 
held the "Mercuries Life Insurance Cup Teeball National Tournament" for 13 consecutive 
years, which is suitable for elementary school children through rooted down the habit 
of exercise to cultivate children's healthy bodies; in conjunction with “Policyholder 
Children's Sketching Competition”, which has been held in 2022, the policyholder is 
encouraged to take their children out for sketching during the holidays, which not only 
enhances parent-child interaction, but also promotes children's physical and mental 
development, hoping to help families raise more healthy and happy children. A total of 
8,585 children participated in the 2022 Teeball and Children's Sketch Competition to 
build a stronger foundation for the development of the country.
 ◆  Organized Taiwan Slow Pitch Softball Father Memorial Cup
It has been held for 18 consecutive years. In 2022, 84 teams and 2,040 players participated 
in the event. The "Mercuries Life Insurance Star Slow Pitch Softball Team" by Mercuries 
colleagues won the Group B Champion in the invitation group.

6.Environmental Influence
Appendix
Mercuries Life Insurance continues to promote enterprise sustainability by calling on 
our employees to participate in public welfare events and focus on more vulnerable 
groups in need of assistance. In 2022, despite the impact of COVID-19, there were still 763 
volunteers, estimated at 3 hours per person, with about 2,289 hours of service in total:
 ◆  Blood donation : Mercuries Life Insurance cooperates with the Taiwan Blood 
Foundation, and holds a quarterly blood donation event every year. In 2022, there were 
86 events across Taiwan and 5,410 blood bags in total. 
 ◆  Environmental protection volunteers : Totally of 7 events, 156 colleagues 
served as volunteers for resource classification at Tzu Chi Environmental Protection 
Education Centre, and went to Changhwa Bank Mountain and Pingtung Dajin Waterfall to 
clean the mountains and protect Taiwan's beautiful environment.
◆  Caring for the vulnerable groups : Totally 7 activities, 274 colleagues 
participated in Genesis Social Welfare Foundation, Shifang Centre, Bade Correctional 
Home for the Disabled, Huashan Social Welfare Foundation and Yate Cup Intellectual 
Disability Games, etc., and also went to the primary school in Ren’ai Village of Nantou 
County for caring indigenous school children. Mercuries Life Insurance has been 
sponsoring the Yate Cup Intellectual Disability Games for more than 20 years to encourage 
students with physical and mental disabilities to show their sporting potential and 
challenge themselves.
Mercuries Life Insurance has responded to the “United Nations Sustainable Development 
Goals (SDGs)” with specific goals and actions, and developed further actions from the 
perspective of corporate strategy and business integration, so as to actively practice 
corporate social responsibility through partnership and the power and influence of

Strategy 
The Company's climate mission is to "support Taiwan and the world to achieve net zero 
emissions by 2050" through the first line of defense to implement climate change risk 
management, identify the financial impact of climate change risks and opportunities on 
business, commodities, investment and loans, and formulate climate-related strategies based 
on assessment results and climate mission. The content is as follows:
A.Climate risk management in investment
As the ESG trend sweeps the world, the Company believes that finance is the blood of 
sustainable growth, and is channeling the money into sustainable growth through green

Governance 
The Company has established a climate governance framework to ensure the 
implementation of climate change risk management through a systematic division 
of responsibilities from the Board of Directors, Risk Management Committee and 
relevant departments of the three lines of defense.
The Board of Directors is ultimately responsible for the administration of climate 
change risks and set up a "Risk Management Committee" to regularly review the 
implementation of climate risk management 
The Risk Management Department shall be responsible for implementing climate 
change risk management-related affairs, and the Head Office shall also ensure that 
the execution results are consistent with the objectives of the Company and ESG, so 
as to guide relevant departments to carry out climate change risk management, and 
report the results to the Risk Management Committee regularly.

Appendix
finance. In order to implement the low-carbon investment, the Company has standardized 
the inclusion of ESG factor in the investment analysis and evaluation process in the 
“Investment Policy" and "Institutional Investor Due Diligence Governance Policy". Prior 
to investment, the Company collects the ESG grade and sustainability report or public 
information of the investment target disclosed by MSCI to understand the implementation 
of its sustainability. After the investment, the Company will fulfill the responsibility of 
management as the investor by negotiating with the enterprise and exercising their 
voting rights. In addition, the Company actively responds to the government's policy on 
investment in key new industries, namely the "Six core strategic industries", including 
green electricity and renewable energy, national defense and strategy, livelihood and war 
readiness, etc. 
B.Green operation
Higher average temperatures under the influence of climate change may increase the 
demand for air conditioning. The Company rates the use of electricity in business premises 
as the main source of carbon emissions in the life insurance industry. The Company adopts 
the method of saving internal energy use and improving energy efficiency to reduce the 
impact of the operation process on the environment, through regular and continuous 
replacement and cleaning of air conditioning unit and equipment room’s indoor unit, 
and replacement of energy-saving lamps to improve the efficiency of use, and achieve the 
purpose of reducing the carbon emissions. At the same time, the Company encourages 
cloud meetings to replace physical meetings, and continues to increase the number of 
locations with video, to reduce the impact on the environment due to personnel travels 
or business trips. Moreover, the Company has actively obtained certification from external 
third-party professional organizations. Since 2016, it has continuously obtained the 
BSI British Standards Institute ISO14001 environmental management system, and also 
completed the 2022 greenhouse gas inventory data confirmation of the province's bases 
simultaneously.
C.Energy management
Under the condition of global warming, the climate change caused by the rising 
temperature of the earth's atmosphere and ocean due to the greenhouse effect which 
not only affects the environment, but also causes ecological damage to animals and 
plants. The Company adheres to the attitude of sustainable operation and fulfills its social 
responsibilities by continuously advocating energy conservation and carbon reduction 
and reducing unnecessary resource consumption. At the same time, the Company's old 
equipment, such as official vehicles and air conditioning equipment, will be replaced in 
a planned manner to reduce carbon emissions. In addition, we continue to invest in and 
evaluate increasing the use of green and solar energies, or planning to purchase related 
green energy to continue to reduce carbon emissions. 
D.Real estate climate risk assessment
Investment real estate: climate change intensifies the frequency of disasters such as heavy 
rainfall and flooding, which may cause physical damage to real estate. In order to prevent 
the risk of accelerated depreciation or loss of real estate, the Company sets inspection 
standards, divides its investment real estate held into different levels of climate risk, and 
adopts corresponding supervision and inspection methods according to different risk 
interpretation to ensure the normal operation of investment real estate and generate long-
term stable returns. 
Loans (real estate collateral): under the influence of climate change, the frequency and 
intensity of extreme climate will increase, so the real estate collateral may suffer from 
flooding. As a result, the value of real estate collateral will be greatly reduced. For purpose 
of effectively grasping the risk of real estate collateral caused by climate change and 
coping with it in advance, the Company will classify the real estate collateral according 
to the flood risk factor, the floor where the collateral is located and the age of the house, 
and take appropriate monitoring measures according to the climate risk level, so as to 
effectively reduce the Company's loan loss probability.
Self-use real estate: under the condition of global warming, global climate change will be 
intensified, and the frequency of floods caused by instant heavy rain will also increase, 
which may cause damage to real estate. In order to prevent the risk of non-use caused 
by damage to self-used immovable property, the Company sets unified inspection 
standards, divides its self-used immovable property into different climate risk levels, and 
adopts corresponding supervision and maintenance methods according to different risk 
interpretations to ensure the normal function of such self-used immovable property, so as 
to maintain a continuous operation
E.Company reputation protection
In case of the Company does not actively adopt carbon reduction transformation 
measures, its reputation may be damaged due to the public's negative impression on 
industries with high climate risks or increased awareness of climate change. Therefore, in 
addition to actively implementing carbon reduction measures, the Company will continue 
to monitor climate-related negative news to ensure that there is no negative impact from 
climate-related risks.
F.Maintain the operation continuity management mechanism
In view of the frequent disasters caused by climate change around the world in recent 
years, the Company has preset a remote office space and computer equipment, 
established the remote home office mechanism, made relevant plans for operation 
continuity, and conducted regular information system backup drills. In addition, the 
Company also positively adopts international standards for continuous management of 
operations and best practices to verify compliance with internal, regulatory and customer 
requirements through independent bodies of its partners, and continuously maintains the 
validity of certificates to ensure its ability to cope with operational disruption risks.

G.Tracking the impact of climate risk on life commodities
Climate risks may affect the frequency or magnitude of the loss of life insurance products. 
Therefore, the Company regularly reviews the claims settlement experience of each 
product, and if such claims settlement experience significantly worsens the situation, it 
may take measures such as repricing or suspension of sale of the product; besides, the 
Company also continues to comply with commodity or actuarial ordinances and practice 
guidelines issued by competent authorities to ensure timeliness and reasonableness in 
responding to climate risks. 
H.Focus on "5+2" policy on investment in key new industries
The Company actively responds to the government's 5+2" investment policy on key new 
industries, including biotechnology and medicine, green energy technology and circular 
economy, and increases the proportion of sustainable investment year by year. In 2021, 
the sustainable investment amount exceeded NT$ 49.74 billion, which even increased 
to NT$ 54.58 billion in 2022. Through low-carbon investment actions, the economy is 
guided to sustainable development. For this, we will support green energy and low-carbon 
investment in related industries to do our part for the environment.
I.Promote low-carbon digital insurance services
Under the trend of the global low-carbon transition, the Company has been providing 
mobile insurance, electronic form, electronic insurance policy, and mobile insurance 
service since 2015. Low-carbon insurance services such as mobile claim settlement. 
Besides, the Company is also continuing to develop diversified low-carbon insurance 
services, and introducing “the Mobile Insurance Service System", "Claim Settlement 
Alliance Chain 2.0", "Electronic Claim Payment Notification" and other service projects 
in 2022 to increase service convenience, improve case handling efficiency and customer 
experience, and reduce paperwork to achieve energy saving and carbon reduction effect. 
In the future, except for optimizing the existing service channels and tools, the Company 
will continue to innovate or cooperate with the authorities to introduce policies, such as 
the "Mobile Insurance Paperless" project, and spare no effort in promoting low-carbon 
digital insurance services.
J.Promote paperless office
Encourage the head office to make good use of OA and check-in system in electronic forms 
and online check-in. With the accumulation of paper files over the years, converting paper 
files to digital files can not only free up physical storage facilities for paper files, but also 
save costs (such as operating costs for ink, toner, paper, postage, manual handling, manual 
management and rent). It can also reduce the burden of many administrative tasks and 
improve work efficiency, thus achieving operational cost savings by creating a low-carbon 
workplace environment.
K.Promote e low-carbon insurance products
As global carbon emissions continue to rise, the resulting air pollution problem poses a 
major threat to the environment and personal health. Considering of this, the Company 
actively promotes green and low-carbon insurance products through providing a brisk 
walking spillover policy and products that encourage policyholders to take more public 
transportation. By reducing renewal insurance premiums through walking or by taking 
public transport, policyholders are provided with double protection. Encourage consumers 
to buy green behaviour products, which will not only reduce insurance premiums and 
improve self-protection, but also encourage consumers to walk more and take public 
transport instead of taking lifts and driving or riding motorcycles, thus achieving carbon 
reduction effect on the environment. In the future, the Company will continue to 
promote more diversified green and low-carbon products, to provide various choices and 
guarantees for consumers, and also to do its part for the environment. 
Risk Management
The Company conducts climate change risk management in accordance with the "Code of 
Practice on Three Lines of Internal Control for Insurance Industry": 
A.First line of defence
Based on TCFD classification, relevant authority and responsibility departments carry out 
the management process of risk identification, measurement, response and monitoring. 
B.Second line of defence
The Risk Management Department assists the first line of defence in identifying, measuring, 
responding to and monitoring climate change risks and implementing necessary 
measures, and the Compliance Office then timely transmits information about relevant 
laws and regulations on climate change risks and urges corresponding authorities and 
accountability units to take necessary measures to comply with.

C.Third line of defence
The Audit Office is responsible for reviewing and assessing the effectiveness of 
internal control and risk management systems designed and implemented by the 
first and second lines of defence in relation to climate change risks, and providing 
recommendations for improvement where appropriate.
Risk identification, risk measurement, risk 
monitoring and exposure status
(1)Risk identification
A.Identify climate risks and opportunities and exposures
The relevant authority and responsibility department of the first line of defence 
identifies the impact degree and potential financial impact of climate risks and 
opportunities on its business scope, and counts the risk exposure of therevious year 
according to the climate risks and opportunities index, which is submitted to the 
risk management department for summary and completion of the "Consolidated 
Table for Climate Risks and Opportunities".
B.Identify the materiality of climate risks
Under the "Guidance on Financial Disclosure of Climate-related Risks for Insurance 
Industry", the insurance industry should set criteria for ranking climate-related risks 
by significance, and prioritize climate-related risks according to material criteria. 
For the "climate transition risk", the level of "greenhouse gas emission" is taken 
as the material standard, and the level of risk on each industrial target of portfolio 
investment is also ranked; in addition, for "climate entity risk", the level of "climate 
change disaster area" is taken as a material criterion, and the level of risk in the area 
where the investment real estate and mortgage object are located is ranked as well.
(A)Materiality criteria and ranking of portfolio investment 
climate transition risks
As shown in the figure below, at the end of December 2022, portfolio exposure to 
high-carbon industries accounted for about 6.03%, among which exposure to oil, 
natural gas and coal products (integrated oil industry, exploration and production) 
was the main exposure, followed by cement manufacturing (cement and aggregate).

Material risk Assessment Outcomes Marketable 
Securities
For securities investment, the relevant units of securities investment shall identify 
industries with high climate risk, and evaluate the industries affected by climate 
risk by referring to the industries or enterprises listed as "Greenhouse Gas Emission 
Inventory and Registration Management Measures and the First Batch of Greenhouse 
Gas Emission Sources That Should Be Inventoried and Registered" by the EPA. The 
materiality of climate risks is further ranked according to identified risk likelihood 
and exposure. The results of the 2022 portfolio climate materiality assessment are 
shown in the figure below, of which the degree of exposure (X-axis) is the amount of 
portfolio investment, while the probability of risk (Y-axis) is the carbon emissions of 
high-carbon industries. On the whole, the carbon emissions and exposure amount 
of oil, natural gas and coal products (integrated oil industry, exploration and 
production) are relatively high with more material risk. 
(B)Climate entity risk materiality criteria and ranking for investment 
real estate and mortgage
For investment real estate and housing loans, the Real Estate and Loan departments identify 
high-climate risk subjects according to the assessment method of the latest version of the 
"Climate Change Flooding Hazard Risk Map" issued by the National Science and Technology 
Center for Disaster Reduction (hereinafter referred to as "NCDR") of the Ministry of Science 
and Technology, and rank disaster risk levels for each region. Exposure degree (X-axis) is 
the value of the subject matter of real estate, while risk occurrence possibility (Y-axis) is the 
average score of the subject matter of NCDR Taiwan flooding disaster risk classification by 
county or city. After evaluating the results of the Company's accounts for investment the real 
estate and housing loans at the end of 2022, as shown in the figure below, and considering 
the value of real estate and the degree of real risk, there is no material real risk for investment 
real estate and mortgage collateral on the whole.

(2)Risk Measurement
According to the TCFD risk classification, risk measurement and response are carried out. Considering 
the availability of situational data, quantitative situational analysis of climate transition risk and climate 
entity risk are carried out only for investment and financing and operating activities. The rest of the 
business activities are characterized by qualitative risk.
A. Investment and financing activities - climate transition risk assessment
In order to mitigate and adapt to the impact of climate change, the governments of all countries have 
declared the vision of net zero and strengthened the control power related to carbon emissions, 
including the EU's "Carbon Border Adjustment Mechanism (CBAM)" and revised “Climate Change 
Response Law" in Taiwan. Greenhouse gas emissions will be reduced through carbon tariffs or charges, 
which may affect the cost or revenue of the investment object. The Company conducts the risk analysis 
for specific industries or investments, taking into account the policy and regulatory factors.
It is assessed that if a carbon fee is imposed in the future, the high-carbon industries will be most 
affected. Therefore, refer to the "Greenhouse Gas Reduction and Management Act" to define the list of 
high-carbon industries (as shown below).
(A)Risk situation analysis of negotiable security transformation
Considering carbon emissions and analysis on temperature paths for climate scenarios, based on the 
climate scenario published by NGFS, and established by central banks and financial regulators around the 
world, the scenario analysis is conducted on the invested companies in high carbon emission industries. The 
operating costs increased by carbon emission tax under the scenarios of orderly transition (Orderly - Zero 
2050) and hot house world (Hot House World - Current Policies) are evaluated respectively. Assuming that 
the target company did not take carbon reduction measures, the future carbon fee of the target company 
was calculated based on the greenhouse gas emissions in 2021 and the global carbon fee parameters for 
2030 and 2050 in the Downscaling REMIND-MAgPIE 3.0-4.4 model.
The Company's bond investments in high carbon emission industries are mainly oil and gas. Under an 
orderly transition scenario, the carbon charge of target companies in oil and gas mining and coal products 
in the years of 2050 is estimated to be up to US $927.09 billion. The overall carbon charge for companies 
investing in high-carbon bonds will be US $944.01 billion. 
Steel manufacturing is the main stock of high carbon emission industries. Under the orderly transition 
scenario, it is estimated that steel manufacturing may bear a total carbon fee of about US$12.46 billion in 
2050. The carbon charge for the overall high-carbon stock investment would be US$14.3 billion.

B.Operating activities - climate transition risk evaluation
(A)Scenario analysis on the risk of operating activities transformation
The electricity consumption of each operation site in 2022 was counted, while carbon emissions were 
converted according to the carbon emission coefficient of electricity in 2021, and the potential financial 
impact of carbon fee imposition in the future was assessed through scenario analysis. According to 
the evaluation, as the Company belongs to the financial and insurance industry, and its main source 
of carbon emission is the power use of office buildings, so there is no significant increase in operating 
costs temporarily assessed. In the future, ISO 14064-1 will continue to be adopted to check the carbon 
emissions among operation sites and promote energy conservation and carbon reduction measures to 
ensure that the operation can meet the regulatory requirements of the competent authorities.
(B)Response to the risk of operating activities transformation
The Occupational Safety and General Affairs Department will take the following measures to 
respond and manage the risk of operation site transformation. 
C. Investment and financing activities - climate entity risk 
assessment
According to the Intergovernmental Panel on Climate Change (IPCC) issued “Impact, 
Adaptation, and Vulnerability" report, human-induced climate change has led to more 
frequent and more intense extreme events, such as extreme rainfall. There will be 
widespread negative impacts on Nature and human, and possibly irreversible impacts. 
The Company conducts the risk analysis of real estate distributions, taking into account 
the extreme weather factors.
(A)Analysis of risk situations of investment real estate and mortgage entities
Considering the carbon emission and temperature paths, the climate scenario analysis 
was conducted, and future flooding hazard risk was also estimated by referring to the 
"Taiwan Disaster Risk Map" of NCDR. The risk level (relative risk) of an area is evaluated by 
considering the hazard (the probability of extreme rainfall), the vulnerability (the extent of 
flooding under specific rainfall conditions) and the exposure (the higher the population 
density, the higher the exposure) for a comprehensively assessing the subject floor and 
the age of house to evaluate the results of scenario analysis on real estate. The entity 
context hypothesis contains the following elements:
▶Risk factor of flooding: According to the "Taiwan Disaster Risk Chart" of the 
National Center for Disaster Prevention and Rescue Technology (NCDR), the future 
flooding risk is divided into Risk1~Risk5 (the higher the value, the higher the risk).
▶Target floor: The risk coefficient below the first floor is 3, the second to the fourth 
floor is 2, and the fifth floor and above is 1.
▶The target age of housing: The risk coefficient is 1for an age of housing more than 
31 years, 2 for 11-30 years, and 1 for less than 10 years.
Risk assessment and classification are carried out according to the subject matter

Results of entity risk assessment on operating sites
D.Operational activity - climate entity risk assessment
(A)Entity risk scenario analysis of operating sites
According to the evaluation, the Company's operation sites are located in all 
counties and cities in Taiwan, and a total of 248 data are recovered. Among 
them, only 3 office work locations are assessed as high Risk, and one of them 
is located in the Zhongshan district of Taipei City, which belongs to the Risk 5 
area defined by NCDR, and is located in a basement with a house age of more 
than 30 years. While other two are located in Jongli district, Taoyuan City, and 
belong to Risk5 as defined by NCDR. They are located on the first floor and the 
first floor of the basement, with a house age is over 30 years.
Formulate continuous operation plans to improve system recovery time 
in response to operational disruptions caused by natural disasters such as 
extreme weather; Regularly assess the impact of natural disasters on operations 
and make improvements based on the assessment results to reduce the risk 
caused by extreme weather events.

(3)Risk monitoring
Take into account the identified climate change risks in 
the development of risk appetite, strategy and operational 
plans, set indexes and targets for climate change risks, and 
continuously monitor their management and disclosure.
A.Risk appetite declaration
The Company's risk appetite statement is: In line with the 
global net zero policy, we will develop strategies, indexes 
and targets to actively manage the risks of climate change 
in order to support the goal of net zero emission by 2050.
B.Risk appetite index
The existing risk appetite index is "IFSR (long-term rating) 
of Taiwan Ratings is no less than twA-", and index control 
is oriented to include the ESG index, among which the 
Environmental index has covered environmental credit 
factors such as climate change risk and entity risk, so 
it can reflect the result of the Company's climate risk 
management ability.
C.Regular monitoring
Relevant departments shall monitor and manage the 
achievements of climate risk/opportunity targets, and 
the risk management department then reports the 
implementation to the Risk Management Committee and 
the Board of Directors.

reduction measures, including e-processes, energy-saving solutions, development 
of energy-saving equipment in green buildings, inventory of greenhouse gas 
emissions at all sites, implementation of environmental management policies, and 
protection of sustainable environment through low-carbon operations.
Promotion of e-documents
In line with the international ESG trend and the pursuit of sustainable 
development of enterprises, and response to the “Green Finance Action Plan 
2.0" promoted by the FSC, the financial institutions are encouraged to develop 
and innovate green financial products or services to meet the financial needs of 
enterprises and investors pursuing the low-carbon transformation and sustainable 
development. By promoting e-documents, Mercuries Life Insurance significantly 
increases the use of electronic policies. In 2022, the "Like Tiger with Electronics" 
promotion activity was launched. During the activity, when the policyholders apply 
for a new contract electronic policy, electronic form, automatic trading service 
and use the automatic specific services (policy loan, withdrawal, conversion, and 
subscription), the points will be accumulated if they meet the requirements, and 
the points will be converted into lucky draw opportunities for policyholders. In 
addition, an e-document promotion team was set up, consisting of the Head Office 
and front-line service personnel, to respond to the operation problems of the 
policyholder at the first moment, assist in promoting a number of e-services and 
integrate channels to give feedback to customers' opinions. Customer problems 
can be responded to and dealt with by service personnel the first time. Customer 
opinions can also be used as suggestions for e-service optimization to improve the 
customer experience.
Our new contract mobile coverage rate reached 97.96% in 2022 to reduce the 
use of about 4.75 million pieces of paper, and indeed decrease the consumption 
of natural resources. In 2022, the number of new contract electronic insurance 
policies will reach 56,656, accounting for 35.28% of the total.
