The policyholder who wishes to pay their premiums through automatic transfer can 
agree on Electronic Direct Debit Authorization(eDDA) at the time of mobile insurance 
and verify their automatic transfer authorization through a chip financial card or 
e-bank. This will not only improve administrative efficiency, but also effectively 
reduce the use of two copies of the authorization form on paper, so as to achieve the 
goal of low-carbon operation.
For the insurance renewal in 2022, the number of premiums paid by automatic 
transfer accounted for 50.54% of the entire effective policies, and the number of 
insurance premiums agreed to be paid by credit card accounted for 31.48% of the 
entire effective policies. In total, the proportion of insurance premiums paid by 
automatic (electronic) payment services was about 82.02% of the entire effective 
policies.

Appendix
Energy Saving Plan
Operating place electricity consumption is the main source of carbon emissions in the life 
insurance industry. In order to reduce the impact of the operation on the environment 
and provide a healthier office environment for employees, by saving internal resources, 
Mercuries Life Insurance reduced energy consumption and environmental pollution. We 
also reduced the carbon emissions by continuously replacing and cleaning the equipment 
and using energy-saving devices, such as regularly cleaning main air conditioners, and 
gradually updating old air conditioner equipment to improve efficiency. At the same 
time, the new workplace also continues to replace energy-saving lamps and lanterns, and 
develops different energy-saving ways through parallel technology and management to 
reduce the excessive use of environmental resources.
Since the 2022 greenhouse gas inventory has expanded the scope of the inventory to 
cover the entire province, and the data has been confirmed, we will use 202216 as the 
base year. From 2016 to 2021, we have successfully reduced the total carbon emissions 
by 40.78%, and set a plan for the next 3 years (to 2024) year) to reduce the total carbon 
emission by 103%, and make the greatest efforts for the sustainable development of the 
environment.
Energy saving settings related to green buildings, such as the Neihu enterprise 
headquarters building, have obtained the "EEWH", and completed the installation of 
solar photovoltaic panel energy saving equipment. Assuming that the average daily 
production of 2.5 degrees /KW in northern part of the country, it is expected to provide 
about 12,154.5 degrees of solar energy per year, with a reduction of 2.3 tons of CO2 per 
1KW, and equivalent to a carbon reduction of 30.6 tons; On the other hand, the Wenxin 
Building in Taichung uses green building materials, such as double glazing and heat-
insulating paper and increasing green space, to show an active action of participating 
in environmental greening and energy saving. Provided that the southern region can 
generate 3 KWH /KW per day on average, it is expected to provide about 17,509.05 KWH 
of solar energy per year, which is converted to a reduction of 2.3 tons of CO2 per 1KW. 
Therefore, it is equivalent to a carbon reduction of 36.8 tons, which can fully supply the 
electricity needed for landscape of the building. 
Energy Use
"In 2022, the Company purchased a new headquarters building, which is equipped with 
energy-saving features that surpass those of the old building, effectively achieving carbon 
reduction goals. Furthermore, considering the energy consumption intensity per unit area 
of the Company's total space, the overall energy usage in 2022 is better than that in 2021. 
The company will continue to implement various energy-saving measures to achieve the 
planned carbon reduction targets.
In Category 3, part of the carbon emissions were calculated based on express fuel. 
This year, we will examine the carbon emissions of our staff traveling by high-speed 
rail and plane. Besides, we are going to expand the use of video equipment, and 
some conferences and educational training will also be launched to promote remote 
connection to reduce the carbon emissions of business travel, which is also part of our 
efforts to control greenhouse gas emissions.

Water Resources Management 
The Company has also set a water saving target, Continue to publicize water-saving measures 
to colleagues, and due to the purchase of a new headquarters building in 2022, the water 
consumption will increase, and due to the slowdown of the epidemic, the number of people 
and time working from home will be reduced, and the water consumption will increase by 
86,200 degrees compared with 2021.
Waste Management 
Wastes generated during the operational process of insurance enterprises are relatively simple 
and have a limited impact on the environment, because the types of waste are only livelihood 
waste and general resource recycling. Nevertheless, we are still committed to implementing 
the resource reuse policy in the process of operation to do the best in waste classification and 
resource recovery. We recycle the papers for reuse, collect the waste batteries centrally, entrust 
the qualified contractors to handle decoration wastes for disposal, and reuse the workplace 
potted plants. As for electronic scraps, we extend their useful lifetime or entrust the contractors 
for recycling and treatment, so as to produce the best possible result through disposing of the 
waster as properly as possible.

In purchasing, we give priority to products with energy saving labels or 
recyclable products, such as computers and screens, environmental toner, etc., 
to reduce carbon emissions in the supply chain. While in purchasing buildings, 
we often prioritize green building labels, and take the lead in replacing old air 
conditioning equipment to reduce the generation of toxic waste.
Green Procurement Amount
Green Procurement
In order to strengthen the sustainable management mechanism of the supply 
chain, the Company uses the “Long-Term Cooperating Supplier Audit Form" 
for evaluation, conducts a field survey of outsourcing suppliers every year 
and issues a visit report to evaluate whether the supplier complies with the 
outsourcing operation specifications. In case where there is any negative 
impression, it is recorded in the “Special Event Table" to be used as a 
reference basis for future sessions of supplier selection. We hope to cooperate 
with suppliers that have ESG concept to achieve the vision of sustainable 
development.

We conduct the pre-examination of the new supplier before cooperation in accordance 
with the six conditions of the “Supplier Selection Principle", including the criterion that 
suppliers shall be qualified established and have contracted business projects, have practical 
experience or ability, guarantee the labor safety and protect the ecology, so as to ensure the 
suppliers meet the Company’s standards in human rights, environment, labor and social 
impact. When the Company engages in the contract execution with a supplier, the supplier is 
requested to sign the “Supplier Ethics and Integrity Undertaking". The Company may rescind 
contracts in case where a supplier violates the Supplier Selection Principle and has dishonest 
behavior.
IT Waste Disposal
Supply Chain Management
We choose to cooperate with local suppliers in priority because we believe that purchase from 
the local suppliers is beneficial to the local economic growth while effectively reducing the 
carbon footprint at the same time. In 2022, there were 19 long-term cooperating suppliers, 
among which there were 8 suppliers in the service category and 11 suppliers in the equipment 
category, and 100% of the suppliers were local suppliers.

Weakness" was continuously launched to help financially troubled policyholders overcome 
difficulties and extended the application period for six months to alleviate the financial 
pressure of them. A total of 167 applications and 194 applications were made, with a total loan 
amount of NT$13,841,877.

reached 97.96%.

Implementation of Principles for Sustainable Insurance (PSI) of the United Nations
Principle 1: Include ESG issues in the insurance company’s decision-making
Issues
Relevant key methods and achievements
Corporate 
strategy
▶Incorporate enterprise sustainability into the annual business plan, and report the implementation progress and effectiveness to the board of directors 
regularly on a quarterly basis.
▶	Set up ethical management, fair customer treatment, regulatory compliance, and other compulsory educational training courses for all staff.
Risk management 
and underwriting
▶Attaches great importance to various ESG risk issues, and continuously evaluates and studies the emerging ESG risks related to climate change, population 
structure change, health care development, and so on.
▶In view of catastrophe events, information security attacks and other risks that may cause significant losses, we have formulated information security 
incident notification and handling procedures, and carried out corresponding level notification and handling operations according to the event level. If the 
event may affect the rights and interests of customers, we will also cooperate with relevant departments of the Company to carry out internal and external 
advocacy to avoid affecting the rights and interests of customers.
▶Conduct regular drills for information security and personal information events to ensure real-time and effective response mechanisms as well as customer 
rights and interests.
▶Carry out various simulation test calculations and commodity, investment and risk control strategy adjustments actively conform to IFRS17 International 
Financial Reporting Standards.
▶In order to implement the principle of equitable hospitality and protect the policyholder rights as well as interests of persons with physical and mental 
disabilities, the Company establishes "Operation Procedures and Notices for New Insurance Contract for Persons with Physical and Mental Disabilities", and 
for persons with physical and mental disabilities, appropriate coverage conditions will be determined by referencing the underwriting evaluation manual 
used by the Company, and coverage shall not be denied without reason.
Sales and 
marketing
▶Promote mobile insurance, mobile online insurance, mobile insurance service, new contract mobile meeting reply, and communicate the concept of energy 
saving and carbon reduction.
▶In the process of product design and sales, we follow the laws and regulations of the competent authorities, and mark the warnings and cautions in 
accordance with the law. 
Product and 
service
▶Respond to government policies, care for vulnerable groups, and promote micro-insurance and small-amount insurance for old age, etc.
▶Continue the financial-related academic research program to exchange the experience.
▶Support for various sports events, and advocate the importance of health risk prevention. 
Claim 
management
▶Provide more efficient claims settlement services through "mobile claims", the use of alliance chain, medical access and digital identity verification 
functions.
▶Provide customer consultation services through the 0800 service hotline, customer service counters in each region, and professional agency force.
▶Notifiable infectious diseases are not included as Exceptions in the insurance products.
▶Provide the policyholder caring measures in the event of major social emergencies and during the epidemic.
Investment 
management
▶ Formulate PRI responsible investment principles and guidelines, which have been approved by the board of directors, and import them into the database to 
improve PRI responsible investment principles.

Principle 2: Raise the awareness of ESG issues, management risks and solution development 
among the customers and business partners
Objects
Relevant methods and achievements
Customers and 
suppliers
▶According to the "Supplier Selection Principle", confirm whether the supplier is qualified to set up and contract the business project, has the practical 
experience or ability, guarantees the labor safety, protects the ecology and does not create pollution, etc., to ensure that the supplier meets the Company's 
standards in the human rights, environment, labor, social impact and other aspects.
▶Require the outsourcing manufacturers to sign the confidentiality agreement, and integrity and anti-corruption commitment.
▶Prefer to choose the local manufacturers with Green Mark that can reduce their carbon footprint in the procurement process. 
Insurers, 
reinsurers and 
brokers
▶Add the anti-money laundering and other related training courses to the cooperative bank channel training courses. 
Principle 3: Promote ESG issues with the government, insurance regulatory authorities and key stakeholders 
Stakeholders 
Relevant methods and achievements
Government 
agencies, 
insurance 
supervisors and 
policy makers
▶Sign the” Code of Due Diligence Governance for Institutional Investors” and perform the due diligence governance report.
▶Promote the corporate governance, fair customer treatment, anti-money laundering, information security and other important issues in accordance with the 
policies of the competent authorities. 
Other key 
stakeholders
▶Participate in the development of TCFD practice manual of climate-related financial disclosure for production and life insurance associations.
▶Commit to the finance and insurance education. For nine consecutive years, sponsor the Risk and Insurance Research Center of National Chengchi University 
to invest in the insurance academic development. For eight consecutive years, sponsor the Fintech Industry-University Cooperation Alliance of National 
Chengchi University (now is the Scientific Research Industrialization Platform of National Chengchi University) to support the fintech innovation. For ten 
consecutive years, cooperate with Modern Insurance Education Foundation to donate for the RMi Magazine.
▶Pay attention to the physical and mental health development of children, and organize "Mercuries Life Insurance Cup Teeball National Tournament" and 
"Policyholder's Children Sketch Competition" for a long time.
▶Blood donation activities are held in four seasons every year, and long-term blood donation activities are also held in autumn and winter to achieve the 
purpose of timely replenishing blood bank feedback to the society.
▶In response to the international public welfare activities of Earth Hour, call on the public to save energy, protect the environment, and love the Earth together 
on the FACEBOOK fan page of Mercuries Life Insurance.
▶Publish the policyholder section periodical on the official website, to provide the insurance concept and health knowledge for policyholders and the general 
public.
Principle 4: Regularly disclose the progress of PSI implementation to achieve the information transparency
Stakeholders 
Relevant methods and achievements
The social mass
▶Issue the sustainability reports and expose them on the Open Information Observatory of the Stock Exchange and the corporate sustainability section of the 
Company's official website.
▶Provide information on ESG strategy and results to clients, investors, rating agencies, etc.

Accountant's Limited Confidence

Accountant's Limited Confidence 
Report 
Summary table of key performance 
indicators
(1) Status of Implementation on Climate-Related Information
Projects
Status of Implementation
1. Clarify the 
Board and 
management’s 
supervision 
and 
governance of 
climate-related 
risks and 
opportunities.
•The Company has established a climate governance structure to ensure the implementation of the climate risk management through a top-down promotion of the board of 
directors, the risk management committee, the risk management department, the chief executive's office, and operating units.
•	 As the highest decision-making unit of climate risk management system, the board of directors is mainly responsible for supervising and managing climate-related risks of the 
enterprise, identifying climate-related opportunities and approving climate risk management measures. The "Risk Management Committee" under the Board of Directors is the 
highest management level of risk management, which convenes meeting once a quarter. In addition to evaluating the operation of risk management systems and reports, it is 
also responsible for formulating climate risk management policies, evaluating the implementation of climate risk management and reporting to the Board of Directors.
•	 Both the Risk Management Department and Executive Office are responsible for coordinating the monitoring, measurement and evaluation of daily climate risks of the Company, 
guiding relevant departments of investment and operation activities of the Company to implement climate risk management business, and regularly reporting management 
results to the Risk Management Committee.
2.Describe how
the identified 
climate 
risks and 
opportunities 
affect the 
business, 
strategy and 
finances of 
an enterprise 
(short, medium 
and long term).
Under the current climate risk management mechanism, the Company carries out the identification of climate risk management by the first line of defense, and measures 
the potential financial impacts on its business, commodities, investment and loans (such as the impact of reduced investment income/operating income, increased operating 
expenses or increased claim expenses) through those identified major risk/opportunity factors. Formulate and implement short -, medium - and long-term coping strategies 
based on evaluation results, and submit relevant implementation results to the risk management committee meeting for review.
3. Identify the
financial
implications
of extreme
climate
events and
transformation
actions
A.Transformation risks:
1.If the investment object belongs to an industry with high climate risk (such as high carbon emission, high energy consumption or high pollution industry), its profitability and 
investment income of the company may be affected by the following circumstances:
(1)Operating costs that increased due to changes in energy regulations, carbon fees and other factors.
(2)As emerging or low-carbon technologies mature, existing products and services are replaced, or carbon reduction processes, energy efficiency or carbon capture and storage 
         technologies are not upgraded, resulting in high costs and negative public perceptions of high-risk industries. 
    (3)With the improvement of public awareness of environmental protection, structural preference changes and demand shifts to green industries.
2.The increased awareness of climate change in the overall atmosphere of society makes the Company have a negative perception due to its investment in the industry with high 
   climate risk.
3.Due to domestic and foreign carbon fee collection and energy policy changes, the Company's electricity expenses and carbon costs have increased.
B.Entity risks:
1.The asset value of real estate investment and related collateral is reduced due to climate disaster events, which affects the asset value impairment and loan guarantee of the 
    Company.
2.Extreme climate disaster events may cause damage to the Company's operating sites or equipment, resulting in disruption of its operations and may reduce operating income 
in addition to increasing repair costs.
3.As for the impact of the physical risk of climate change on life insurance products, the Company still needs to keep observing and analyzing because there is no specific and 
modelable conclusion in relevant studies.
C.In view of the transformation risk and entity risk, relevant authorities have developed strategies to mitigate the possible financial impact on the Company.
Execution of climate-related information by listed OTC companies

(1) Status of Implementation on Climate-Related Information
Projects
Status of Implementation
4.	 Explain how climate 
risk identification, 
assessment and 
management processes 
are integrated into the 
overall risk management 
system. 
The Company has incorporated climate change risks into the "Risk Management Policy" and formulated the "Climate Change Risk Management 
Approach" for control. In the implementation of climate risk management as the first line of defense, the Company also analyzes the association 
between various risk factors and existing risks and establishes their links to integrate them into the overall risk management system.
5.	 Where scenario analysis 
is applied to assess 
resilience to climate 
change risks, the context 
applied, parameters, 
assumptions, analysis 
factors and key financial 
implications should be 
explained 
A.Entity risks:
Referring to the future flooding disaster risk estimated by the National Disaster Prevention and Rescue Science and Technology Center (NCDR) in 
“Taiwan Disaster Risk Map”, the risk level (relative risk) of a region is evaluated by considering the hazard degree (probability of extreme rainfall), 
vulnerability degree (flooding range under specific rainfall conditions) and storm risk degree (the higher the population density, the higher the storm 
risk), as well as a comprehensive assessment on the subject floor and house age.
B.Transformation risks:
With reference to the climate scenario published by NGFS, a scenario analysis of invested companies in high carbon emission industries is carried out. 
Besides, the increased operating costs due to carbon expenditure under the scenarios of Orderly-Net Zero 2050 and Hot House World-Current Policies 
were also evaluated respectively.
1.Securities
    Make an inventory of greenhouse gas emissions of the investment target company to introduce scenario analysis and estimate the carbon expenses 
    that the Company may face in the future; It is assessed that under the orderly transition scenario, the investment target companies with high overall 
    carbon emissions in 2050 will have high carbon expenses.
2.Operational sites
    Check the electricity consumption of each operation site, and convert carbon emissions according to the carbon emission coefficient to import a 
    situation analysis. As assessed, the Company belongs to the finance and insurance industry, and its main source of carbon emissions is the 
    electricity use of office buildings, and there is no significant increase in operating costs.
6.	 If there is a 
transformation plan 
to manage climate-
related risks, describe 
the plan and the targets 
and objectives applied 
to identify and manage 
entity and transformation 
risks
The contents, indicators and objectives of the Company's plan to manage entity and transformation risks are highlighted as follows:
A.Conduct climate risk management and audit of investment business based on TCFD framework, and in the early stage of PCAF introduction, the 
    portfolio proportion covered by inventory shall reach 80% as a goal.
B.Monitor the Company's exposure to high-carbon emission industries or enterprise investment risks, and conduct a climate risk assessment on the 
    investment objects of medium-high climate risk industries under the investment portfolio, with the initial assessment ratio of 95% as a target.
C.Reduce greenhouse gas emissions from its operations, aim to reduce cumulative carbon emissions by 3% in 2024 compared with the base year, and 
    expand the scope of ISO 14064-1 certification from the head office to all operating sites.
D.Continuously monitor and actively respond to negative news related to the Company's climate risk management. 
E.For the real estate with high climate risk held by the Company, protective measures (such as flooding prevention equipment) will be evaluated, 
    and entity risk assessment items will also be added to the real estate questionnaire with a case assessment ratio initially targeted at 50%.
F.Continue to track domestic laws and regulations related to climate risk of life insurance products and research to assess the impact of climate risk     
    on life insurance products and future trends.
G.Continually strengthen the Company's continuous management mechanism for natural disaster-related operations and obtain relevant 
    certification  (ISO 22301), handle at least one regular drill backup and recovery plan every year (recovery time efficiency is less than 24 hours/time), 
    to ensure that the Company can resume operation as soon as possible when facing related accidents.

7.In case of internal carbon 
pricing is adopted as a 
planning tool, the price 
setting basis should be 
explained. 
The Company had not yet used internal carbon pricing as a strategic management tool for climate change risk in 2022. 
8.	If climate-related 
targets are set, 
information should 
be provided on the 
activities covered, the 
scope of greenhouse 
gas emissions, the 
planning period and 
the yearly progress in 
achieving them; and on 
condition that carbon 
credits or renewable 
energy credits (RECs) 
are applied to achieve 
relevant objectives, the 
source and quantity of 
credits or the number 
of renewable energy 
credits (RECs) should be 
stated.
The Company makes an inventory of carbon emissions generated by Scope 1, Scope 2 and Scope 3 (employee travel) at all locations.
The short-term target is set to reduce carbon emissions by 1% per year, and the medium-term target is set in 2030, hoping to achieve 
a target of 10% reduction. With the rapid development of science and technology and the mature development of the green energy 
industry, it is expected to achieve the government's long-term goal of net zero carbon emission in 2050.
9.	Greenhouse gas 
inventory and assurance 
status 
From 2023, expand the inventory of the province's business bases for 2022 of greenhouse gas inventory and confirmation, and report 
to the board of directors on a quarterly basis for the inventory plan and progress description.
